Liang's Division Recovers Geyuan 98

Geyuan is a Base for Bandits on the Borders of Jiangxi, Fujian, Zhejiang, and Anhui

It Will Not Be Difficult to Sweep Away the Remnant Bandits Retreating Towards Dexing

Nanchang Communication: Geyuan belongs to Hengfeng and can connect to Chong'an in Fujian via Qianshan in the south, reach the Xin River via Yiyang in the west, and is intertwined with the border of Rao in Yushan and Zhejiang in the east. It is closely connected to Dexing in the north, remotely connecting to Wuyuan and Qimen, and the terrain is high, steep, and difficult to attack. Therefore, after the bandit Fang Zhimin's birthplace, Mobanshan, was broken by Lu Xiaochen's troops in the 19th year, he used Geyuan as his only base. Important institutions such as the pseudo Northeast Revolutionary Committee, the pseudo Jiangxi-Zhejiang-Anhui Military Region Headquarters, and the pseudo Jiangxi-Zhejiang-Anhui Provincial Government were all located there. Even institutions such as the pseudo Post Office, the pseudo Arsenal, and the pseudo Agricultural and Industrial Bank were painstakingly managed. For several years, the bandits in eastern Jiangxi, northern Fujian, western Zhejiang, and southern Anhui have taken this as their command center. Previously, Chairman Chiang appointed Chen Diaoyuan as the Commander-in-Chief of the Five-Province Bandit Suppression Reserve Army, supervising Zhao Guantao, Yu Jishi, and others to command the armies of Jiangxi, Zhejiang, and Anhui to encircle and suppress the bandits, also taking Geyuan as the goal of their meeting. Its importance on the borders of the three provinces is like Ruijin on the borders of Jiangxi, Guangdong, and Fujian. Since the joint suppression by the troops of Tang Huiyuan, Liang Lizhu, Yu Jishi, and Ruan Zhaochang, Hengfeng has been recovered, but the bandits have retreated to a corner of Geyuan, still maintaining their last base. Another part of the bandit army, along with the pseudo Ninth Army and Luo Binghui's troops, fled to Fujian, Zhejiang, Anhui, and Jiangxi, making circular movements, hoping to expand the guerrilla area and disperse the national army's suppression forces, as an attempt to cut off the water at the base of the cauldron for Hengfeng and Geyuan. After the national army inflicted heavy damage on the bandits in Zhejiang on the border of Zhejiang by Zhao Guantao and Yu Jishi, the bandits on the border of Anhui were intercepted by Chen Diaoyuan's troops, and the scattered bandits in Fuliang and Dexing were severely attacked by Li Zongjian's troops. Geyuan was attacked and captured by Liang Lizhu's troops of the 21st Division. Since last year, starting from Hekou, they have launched an upward attack, advancing in the overlapping mountains with bunkers and highways alternately, like grinding ink. After dozens or hundreds of battles, they approached Geyuan last month. At that time, the pseudo Tenth Army's 83rd Regiment, 87th Regiment, and Shangrao Pseudo Independent Battalion, which guarded the nest, took Geyuan as the core of the bandits, and built densely packed and heavily stacked fortifications on the surrounding mountains and strategic passes to resist stubbornly. However, the national army's Lu Regiment bravely climbed, charged upwards in hand-to-hand combat. The Gan Regiment also led troops to advance fiercely at the same time, and finally broke through the bandit bunkers and fortifications, completely recovering Geyuan on November 28th. The Overseas Chinese Northeast Military Region Headquarters, the pseudo Fujian and Zhejiang Provincial Government, the pseudo Red Army Fifth Branch School, the pseudo Shangrao County Government, the pseudo New Communist Training Center, the pseudo Agricultural School, the pseudo Postal Administration, various pseudo party headquarters, pseudo Economic Committees, and other institutions were completely destroyed. The remnant bandits retreated northward towards Dexing. In addition to telegraphing □□□ troops to intercept them, Liang's Division is currently searching for remnant bandits, searching for weapons buried by bandits, repairing fortifications, sheltering refugees, and handling the aftermath to stabilize society. The base of the Red bandits on the borders of the three provinces has been lost, and it will not be difficult to eliminate the scattered bandits that are separated and lurking by combining suppression and appeasement. (December 1st)

After the Recovery of Bandit Areas in Jiangxi Province 99

Material Shortages Are Being Actively Addressed

Nanchang Correspondence: After the Red bandits abandoned their base areas of seven or eight years and fled west en masse, all the bandit areas have been successively recovered by the National Army. However, after the devastation of the bandit areas, all necessities of life are being supplied by the rear. The most lacking and necessary items in the bandit areas are briefly described below:

Medicine 100

Since the bandit areas were blockaded, no Chinese or Western medicines flowed in at all. Although a small amount was occasionally obtained through guerrilla warfare or secret attacks, only high-ranking military officers who were seriously injured or ill could benefit. The rest of the soldiers mostly used herbal and folk medicines for treatment. Many wounded soldiers in the bandits' so-called rear hospitals died from festering wounds and maggots. Therefore, in various places recovered by the National Army, sick soldiers and refugees are everywhere. Various medicines are available for money but not on the market. The rescue and treatment teams organized by the Ministry of Health and the Jiangxi Provincial Health Department have dispatched fifteen teams to be stationed in Ruijin, Jinxi, Yudu, Xingguo, Shicheng, Guangchang, Xiaosong, Baishui, and Xin'an. The dying and abandoned who seek treatment are as if returning to the marketplace.

Cotton 101

The bandit areas neither produce cotton nor import cloth. Ruijin, being the bandits' capital, previously had coarse cloth selling for several dimes per foot. When the bandits retreated, they took every last thread. The old and weak who did not leave were barely covered, and those who escaped from the bandit ranks were also in tattered clothes. In the severe winter, many refugees are in single layers. The head of the Department of Civil Affairs, having witnessed this miserable situation on the front lines, returned and convened an emergency meeting by the provincial government to launch a campaign to solicit winter clothing. Mobilization and solicitation have been carried out in various schools, chambers of commerce, and party headquarters, and tens of thousands of cotton-padded garments have been raised. These have been distributed to various counties such as Ruijin, Shicheng, Xingguo, and Yudu. The Provincial Suppression Committee and the Provincial Party Headquarters are still continuing to solicit donations from other counties.

Rice Grain 102

All able-bodied men in the bandit areas were drafted into the bandit army, leaving no one to cultivate the land. Moreover, after the land was divided, the rice grain obtained by the farmers was heavily taxed by the pseudo-township Soviet governments, leading to wasteland overgrown with weeds knee-high. Rice grain production decreased, while the bandits' consumption increased daily. In various districts newly recovered by the National Army, no one has a surplus of even a dipper of grain. Military officers stationed in Yudu, Xingguo, and other places have telegraphed the province requesting the transport of rice for relief. However, transportation is extremely difficult. For example, transporting rice from Nanchang to Yudu costs thirty-six yuan. It is said that the Agricultural Bank and the former Food Administration will be used to transport the rice grain stored in Linchuan, Ji'an, Taihe, and other places for relief. The famine situation is particularly severe in various places in southern Jiangxi, requiring urgent attention. The situation is slightly better on the upper reaches of the Fu River and along both banks of the Gan River.

Salt 103

Since the strict implementation of the blockade, people in areas bordering the bandit areas have been purchasing two qian of salt and lamp oil daily with public sale permits, so no amount leaks into the bandit areas. Only in areas near the Fujian and Guangdong borders, such as Huichang and Yudu, can small amounts be smuggled in through various means, costing several liang per yuan. After the National Army recovered various places, the people, having not eaten salt for a long time, often have swollen heads and faces. Recently, a large quantity of salt has been transported by truck to Ningdu, Yudu, Huichang, and Shicheng for emergency relief. Xingguo will hold a salt distribution. When the Sixth Route Army held a military-civilian gathering in Longgang, several liang of salt were distributed to each person, and everyone rejoiced as if they had obtained a treasure.

Able-Bodied Men 104

The population of the bandit areas has decreased dramatically due to continuous warfare and escape. During this westward flight of the Red bandits, in addition to those already enlisted in the bandit army, all able-bodied men who could move were coerced to the west by the bandits. In the newly recovered districts, there are only a few old, weak, sick, or more women than men. Even healthy women have been conscripted into propaganda and comfort teams. In the future, the only solution will be to immigrate and cultivate wasteland.

Ironware 105

The oxen and livestock of the farmers in the bandit areas have long been slaughtered and eaten. Even the farmers' iron tools such as plows, hoes, and spades have been melted down by the bandits for use as weapons and spears. The replenishment of iron tools and farming implements in the future will also become a major problem. (November 29th)

Northwest Inspection Notes

Special Correspondent of This Newspaper, Geng Ya

Malianjing, Where Vegetation Is Lush 106

Daquan is one station away from Malianjing and two stations away from Xingxing Gorge. Due to waiting for the escort team, we stayed in Daquan on the 11th and did not move forward. It was not until noon on the 12th that the escort team arrived, and we set off immediately and reached Malianjing.

In recent years, traffic between Anxi and Hami has been relatively peaceful due to the efforts of the troops stationed in the two cities. The robbery at Xingxing Gorge was indeed unexpected. After receiving the reporter's letter, Ma Shou-xuan, commander of the Anxi Ma Regiment, believed that the incident was related to the duties of the garrison. In addition to dispatching company adjutant Han Zhan-yuan and soldiers Ma Er-gong and others, seven people in total, to bring dry rations and weapons and come day and night to escort them out of the border, he also sent two cavalry teams to Masonsan and Dunhuang to prevent the bandits from carrying the stolen goods away. Han and Ma carried a military telephone and borrowed the new Gansu telegraph line to talk directly to Commander Ma of Anxi. He learned that he had telegraphed Dr. Yao Le, commander of the Hami garrison, who had also sent troops east to welcome and escort them. Everyone was delighted.

We set off from Daquan, the land was flat, and the weather was clear. After traveling about twenty li, we suddenly encountered a violent cold wind with snowflakes flying. Although it stopped after a moment, the wind became colder and stronger, so that even heavy fur coats were not warm, and the lips were stiff and difficult to speak. Sitting high on the camel, the cold was truly unbearable. At that time, the camels were just starting their journey, fat and tall, walking with broad strides and steady gaits. Riding in the cold was quite difficult. Unexpectedly, when passing a stone gorge, the camel ridden by Mr. Su took a big step and suddenly threw Mr. Su to the ground, his wrist bleeding profusely. However, due to the cold, not much blood flowed and soon congealed like pine resin, but it was still painful. The camel sedan that the reporter was riding in was made of ropes and felt, and one camel could carry two people, which was relatively warm. However, it was a pity that we could not communicate with the seated Shang Mu-sha. Seeing that Mr. Su was injured, I specially exchanged rides with him to help him recover. Later, the wind grew stronger, and the cold increased. The reporter sat sideways to avoid the wind for more than ten li. Unexpectedly, the oilcloth he was carrying broke, and the wind blew it away. The camel was startled and ran away. The reporter was thrown down again, fortunately on the sandy ground, and only his buttocks were slightly sore. Getting up and doing some exercise, the camel driver smiled embarrassedly and said, "A donkey falls lightly, a horse falls heavily, but when a camel falls, even if you have a life, you won't move. That you can still do foreign exercises at this moment is really everyone's luck." Later, he changed to riding a donkey, and finally safely arrived at Malianjing, a distance of seventy li, and the wind also stopped suddenly.

The hardship of riding a camel had been experienced before in the grasslands of Inner Mongolia. This time, because there were no cars or horses, (from Su to Xinjiang, there used to be high-wheeled carts pulled by five horses, in which one could sit or lie down, but now there are none. If riding mules and horses, the exposed fodder would require two more horses to carry, which is also quite troublesome), we rekindled our relationship with camels. Although we were thrown down today, we have learned four things to pay attention to when riding camels: (1) You must ride the head camel because it is docile and the camel driver can pull it, making it less likely to be dangerous. The other camels following behind are bound to become increasingly fierce. (2) The camel driver is responsible for properly securing the luggage, as well as tightening the saddle and bellyband (camel transport does not usually use a bellyband), and then holding the saddle rope and sitting upright on it. You must not imitate the camel driver by climbing up and down the neck, and you must not sit sideways or lie down freely. (3) When getting on and off, you must wait for the camel to lie down firmly before moving. (4) It is best to still use a camel sedan, so that the elderly and women can be safe. Sitting in it is more comfortable for rain and convenience than riding a horse.

Malianjing used to have village houses and temples, but they have all disappeared. The postman's residence, three earthen houses with red willow woven doors, can still barely provide shelter from the wind and rain. Looking out over the flat fields, yellow grass grows densely. Areas with saline-alkali soil can all be reclaimed into farmland. When asked, "Why is there no one to cultivate them?", the answer was that wells must be dug very deep before reaching the water source. The so-called "very deep" initially seemed to be a metaphor using a horse stick or ox rod, short being two or three chi, and long being no more than five chi. Later, seeing the depth of each well, it did not exceed what was expected. If we can emulate the method of digging wells for irrigation in Shandong, immigrate and cultivate land, and engage in large-scale operations, then the barren land can immediately be turned into fertile soil, and the abandoned ruins can become strong defenses.

There are many kinds of shrubs and weeds here. Walking around and collecting them, we quickly obtained more than thirty kinds. The camel driver knew the local names of more than twenty kinds: red willow, also known as Guanyin willow, four or five chi high, with spike-shaped red flowers, small and dense branches and leaves, and old trunks coiled on the ground; white thorns, with branches and trunks that are strong and white, densely covered with small granular leaves and sharp thorns; yellow wood head, with old trunks that are short and thick, densely covered with yellow-green branches, seemingly without flowers or leaves; Bawangchai is quite similar to white thorns, but coarser and without thorns; Shenghun branches and trunks are like vines, very tough, and can be used to pierce camel noses (the above are shrubs).

Achnatherum splendens sprouts new seedlings in the spring, the same as ordinary grass, withers in the winter but does not decay, three or four chi high, white in color, and tough. It can be used to weave cool hats and baskets. If you encounter a solid one, it can also be used as chopsticks. The "Book of Han" mentions "one-breath chicken grass." Cen Shen's poem "The north wind rolls the ground" [one break of white grass] all refers to this grass. Trowel-leaf grass has leaves that are yellow and shaped like trowels, and looks like scissors or hooks. The growth is similar to cactus. Camel thorn has leaves like locust trees, but they are not compound, the branches are lush, and the thorns are sharp. Camels like to eat it. Tobacco-like plants have opposite compound leaves, smaller than fingernails. They can be mixed with real tobacco and smoked. Astragalus chrysanthus of the chrysanthemum family has flowers that curl inwards after shedding, shaped like bone protuberances, but they smell bad and cannot be used as feed. Malian grass has flowers and leaves like orchids, also called Malan grass, with purple-blue flowers that are very beautiful. The pods split and explode. Also false orchids. Camel hoofs are of the amaranth family, with thick and fleshy leaves shaped like camel hoofs. Red sand cork has branches and leaves similar to artemisia, and small pink flowers that are also very beautiful. Reeds are the same as those grown in the interior, but not tall and fertile. Zhaolaojiao has broad, sprawling leaves, small white flowers, and fruits like goat horns. The inner seeds are flat grains of brown color. After the sharp ends of the fruits split, the seeds fly away with the wind. Grain-leaf grass has stems and leaves that are drooping like rice ears, with a lot of moisture. Grass of the genus Agropyron, in the grass family, is a type of wild wheat. Lalajiang has tall branches and stems, and autumn leaves like wax, with beautiful white inflorescences. Diqianjiang, also known as sweet radish, has long and wide leaves and thick roots, with a sweet and sour taste. Sea cypress, in the artemisia family, has branches and leaves like cypress, green in summer and red in autumn, adding to the beauty of the desert landscape. It contains saline moisture and sometimes reveals saltpeter on the outside. Gray strips and white artemisia, yellow artemisia, etc., are also produced in the interior (the above herbs can be used for feed). In addition, there are important medicines such as elephant ear leaves, which are wide and large and look like elephant ears, with flowers like herbaceous begonias that are extremely beautiful, as well as plantain, rhubarb, ephedra, licorice, fragrant artemisia, yinchen, and Suoyang, all of which are abundant.

Suoyang is a holy medicine for tonifying yang. Soldier Ma Er-gong inadvertently dug up three branches while burying telephone ground lines. After peeling off the scaly red skin, a pink color was initially revealed, as thick as an infant's wrist. The inner texture is tender and crisp, quite like sweet potatoes. Chewing it raw is sweet and slightly astringent. At that time, a postman named Niu was nearby, and he dug up several more branches by digging in the cracked ground, which were even thicker than before. The postmen at nearby stations do not farm or harvest, and the only vegetable they have is Suoyang, which they shred and steam with noodles, and the taste becomes purely sweet. Other things like licorice and ephedra are even cut and used as firewood, and no one has yet used them for medicinal purposes. This is probably a mistake due to the misconception that "deserts are barren."

Songjiang 107

Discovery of a Dead Man on the Road in Zhangzhuang

Yesterday, a dead man was found on the road in Zhangzhuang, Twenty-first Ward, near Shihudang. He was wearing a gray wool serge robe, gray wool serge pants, and gray wool serge shoes. The township police of the ward reported it to the county court. The court prosecutor, along with an autopsy clerk, conducted an examination and determined that the death was due to natural causes. However, the deceased was nearly thirty years old. What caused his tragic death and who his family members are will only be known after a public notice is issued to claim the body, and an investigation will then begin.

Hooligan Bandit Xiao Gen, Executed by Firing Squad in Nanhui 108

The hooligan bandit Liu Genfa (also known as Xiao Genfa), a native of Tangjiao Mouth in this county, colluded with Mao Muxiang and Liu Aluan, who had previously been executed, to repeatedly rob and injure people and kidnap people for ransom in the coastal areas of this county, committing numerous crimes. He was wanted for arrest but had not been apprehended. Recently, the suspect robbed the Penglai Bank in the Penglai Market in Shanghai in collaboration with others. After the case was discovered, he was arrested under the alias Li Ziyun. After investigation by the county government, he was escorted back from the Shanghai District Court. The victims Pan Genlou, Pan Xuelin, Mao Zhuqing, and Mao Quanlou were summoned to identify him. It was confirmed that the suspect was indeed guilty of robbery and kidnapping. It was also found that Mao Muxiang, Liu Aluan, and others had originally testified that the suspect was indeed one of the ringleaders. The county government had sentenced him to death, and the sentence was submitted to the Jiangsu Provincial Government for approval by telegram. Yesterday morning at ten o'clock, the suspect was taken to court, where trial judge Jiang confirmed his identity and escorted him to the execution ground outside the South Gate, where he was executed by firing squad.

Villagers in Suzhou Riot, Burn Houses, and Resist Rent 109

Villagers in Xietang and Kuatang outside Suzhou previously used unfair wasteland surveys as an excuse to vent their anger on rent collectors, gathering crowds to burn down dozens of the rent collectors' houses, causing a huge disturbance. After the government sent troops to suppress the riot, it was quelled. Recently, landlords and merchants have been rushing to collect rent. Unexpectedly, on the second day, the houses of rent collector Wu Tongquan in Linjiagang, Jiaozhi Township, and the houses of rent collectors Sun Qiutao, Sun Tingtao, and Sun Qiucha, and the house of Xing Ronggen in Yaobang, and the house of Jiang Rongfu in Luxiang were again set on fire by villagers, destroying more than sixty houses in four villages and six families, resulting in huge losses. The villagers dispersed at dawn. After the incident, the Sixth Branch of the Public Security Bureau sent police to arrest them, but it was too late. The farmers involved in the incident were not local farmers but came from Xietang, Chefang, and other places. After hearing the report, the county government immediately sent the Seventh Security Brigade to suppress the riot and investigate and arrest the ringleaders. After the security team arrived in the township, they deployed defenses in each village to prevent any accidents. The county government has already reported to the provincial government for instructions. As for the issue of rent payment by the farmers, discounts and concessions have been resolved, but very few have paid their rent. An investigation revealed that someone was preventing them from doing so. Yesterday (the fourth), a passenger surnamed Su, who was traveling on a Suzhou-Changzhou bus, said that when the bus passed Weijingtang outside Qimen, he saw farmers disembark to investigate. They saw villagers coming to the city to pay rent and firmly persuaded them to go ashore and postpone the rent payment. The situation seemed to indicate that someone was instigating rent resistance. It is not clear whether it is related to the burning of the rent collectors' houses. Furthermore, more than one hundred farmers, including Yang Guichun from Nanguo, submitted a petition to the county government, accusing rent collector Jiang Rongfu of falsely reporting wasteland, engaging in embezzlement and bribery, and harming others for personal gain. They requested an investigation and a reassessment to ensure fairness.

Rampant Banditry in Four Townships of Wuxian County 110

Since the beginning of winter, robberies have been frequently heard in the four townships, and even in the well-defended urban areas, there have been three cases of robbery and injury. According to news reports, the house of Xu Genjin, a villager in Miaojinbang Township, Lieshu, was visited by seven bandits on the night of the third, who robbed him of more than one hundred yuan in silver and clothing. On the morning of the third, a bandit boat arrived in Tangjiaxiang, Lumu Township, carrying more than ten bandits, who landed and robbed. The victims included He Gaosheng and Yin Zhou, who lost more than three hundred yuan. The bandit boat arrived in Zhanggeng, Huangdai Township, and more than ten bandits rushed into the house of Zhang Longfu, searched arbitrarily, and went to Xihedang. On the dawn of the fourth, the house of farmer Zhu Ronggui in Xishan Township, along Taihu Lake, was robbed by bandits, who kidnapped Zhu Ronggui's eight-year-old son, Agou, before leaving.

Rise in Theft Cases in Wuxi After the Drought 111

After this year's drought, the poor had no clothes or food, leading to a surge in theft cases. In the past two nights, several robberies occurred in urban and rural areas. Excerpts are as follows: (1) Baoshun Credit Union's fast boat, traveling from Wuxi to Suzhou, was passing Hongmiaotou when a boat from Jiangbei suddenly approached. Six bandits jumped out with a pistol and robbed six yuan in letters and two yuan and ninety cents in change. The boat had to turn back. (2) A wonton shop owner in Jiangxi Bridge, Second District, was robbed of four yuan by bandits in Yupu Temple. Another villager's family nearby was robbed of rice and grain carts. None of them have reported the incidents to the police. (3) Wang, the wife of Shao Renhong, a resident of Wuxi, was returning home from watching a play at Qingsheng last night. On the way, her handbag was snatched, resulting in a loss of nine yuan.

Maid Abandoned After Master-Servant Affair, Commits Suicide 112

At about 4 p.m. on the (3rd) of the day before yesterday, a young female guest, about twenty years old, arrived at the City Park Hotel and booked room 43 on the third floor. The guest registration card showed her name as Zhou Yufen, from Heqiao, and she paid the room fee. At about 6 p.m., she went out once in person, bought 200 wen worth of sorghum wine, and drank it in the room to the point of intoxication. Then she took off her clothes and went to sleep. At about 10 p.m., tea servants Chen Arong and Shen Ayi entered the room to check on her, as they were concerned that the female guest might vomit while drunk and soil the bedding. Unexpectedly, they saw that Yufen's expression had changed and her breathing was short. Realizing that something was wrong, they reported it to the front desk and had her carried to the Brothers Hospital for treatment. According to Dr. Zhu's diagnosis, Yufen had taken sleeping pills and raw opium, and had swallowed them along with sorghum wine, resulting in severe poisoning and little hope of survival. He reported it to the First Police Station, and police were dispatched to investigate. It was then learned that Yufen was a maid in the home of Dr. Zhu. Two suicide notes were recovered, one addressed to her mother and one to her master and mistress. The notes contained many hidden feelings, and the reason for the suicide seemed to be an affair with the master, which led to her being abandoned.

Nantong Avoids Conflicts Between Tax Police and Salt Consumers 113

Tax police in the Huainan-Tong area have had conflicts with salt consumers when inspecting salt, resulting in bloody incidents. Yi Ziqi, director of the Fourth Tax Police District, reported to various circles on the 3rd that three measures have been decided to avoid conflicts: (1) Strictly prohibit collusion between officials and thugs and strictly limit searches of salt consumers' homes. (2) Eliminate the source of smuggled salt by transferring rear troops to the producing areas. (3) Various circles will jointly establish a salt consumption cooperative to increase tax revenue and eliminate smuggled salt.

Sea Bandits Swarm to Yangzao Again 114

Coastal bandit boats in the Tong area, which had previously been repelled by the water police, were joined on the 3rd by five large bandit boats from Qidong, with more than 300 bandits, swarming on the Yangzao sea. There was a tendency to land, and the county government has transferred troops to suppress them.

Sudden Cold Weather in Gaoyou, River Freezes 115

Since the beginning of winter, the weather in this county has been mild, without any signs of severe winter. Unexpectedly, after the northwest wind yesterday, the climate suddenly turned cold, and the thermometer dropped to 38 degrees, and only 34 degrees outdoors. This morning (the 2nd), the water has frozen into thin ice, and the poor people who have no clothes or food are all crying in misery.

The Opium Paste Business Is About to Begin 116

The Maoxing Opium Paste Business in this county purchased 4,000 taels of opium paste from the province and transported it by mail. Liu, the section chief of the Prohibition Committee, supervised the opening of the seal. The opium paste of the Dacheng Opium Paste Business is also about to arrive by mail. It was originally scheduled to start business yesterday (the 1st), but due to incomplete procedures, it will be officially opened within a few days. The County Prohibition Committee has specifically ordered the opium paste shops in each district to purchase it as soon as possible and report the opening address, otherwise, it will be reported to the province to revoke the license and invite other merchants to take over the business.

Manager of Haining Agricultural Bank Accused 117

Gu Dayi, the manager of the Haining County Farmers' Bank, was recently accused by citizens Pang Zheng and Wu Shichao in successive reports to the Provincial Department of Construction. It is said that the accusations include violating regulations, engaging in embezzlement and bribery, misappropriating bank funds, using aliases and shadow accounts, and using empty goods as collateral. After receiving the report, the Provincial Department of Construction has sent Luo Chuying to Haining to investigate.

League of Nations Two Experts Arrive in Shanghai Yesterday 118

Visited the Greater Shanghai Construction Project in the Morning, Visited Song (Ziwen) in the Afternoon

Head to Hangzhou This Morning, then to Inspect Water Conservancy and Transportation Nationwide

Complete Work in Three Months, Draft Plans to Contribute to Our Country

丨Two More Experts to Arrive in China One After Another After the 15th丨

Huadong News Agency reports: In order to implement technical cooperation with our country in economic construction, the League of Nations has successively selected expert consultants to come to China to assist our country's plans, improve various industries, and economic construction. Those who have already arrived in China include silk expert Dr. Mari and consultant Bourdvez, etc. Last month, in order to improve our country's water conservancy and river works, the League of Nations specially selected four experts to come to China to investigate water conservancy, highway, and other projects. These four people are: ㈠ Good, a member of the London Institution of Civil Engineers; ㈡ Coursin, Director of the Public Works Department of Madagascar, a French territory in Africa; ㈢ Nie Yufu, reporter of the League of Nations Transportation and Public Works Committee and consultant engineer in The Hague, Netherlands; ㈣ Omades, reporter of the League of Nations Transportation and Public Works Committee and consultant engineer in Milan. Now, Mr. R. Coursin and Mr. A. Omades arrived in China from Geneva on the seventh of last month. Coursin traveled on the Italian ship "Conte Verde" and Omades traveled on the French ship "Aramis," arriving separately. The two ships arrived simultaneously yesterday. Qin Fen, Secretary-General of the Economic Committee, represented Guo Dehua, and Kang Shizhen, representative of the Highway Department of the Committee, went to meet them. After disembarking, they stayed at the Cathay Hotel. The two gentlemen, Coursin and Omades, inspected the construction situation of Greater Shanghai in the morning and visited Song Ziwen, a member of the Standing Committee of the Economic Committee, in the afternoon. It was decided that they would depart by car at eight o'clock this morning to Hangzhou, then to Beijing, and then to the whole country to inspect river water conservancy, highway traffic conditions, and then seek improvement plans. The details are as follows:

Welcoming Personnel 119

Those who went to the Pudong Wharf yesterday morning to welcome them included Guo Dehua, representative of Qin Fen, Secretary-General of the National Economic Committee; Kang Shizhen, Technician of the Highway Department of the Committee; Mr. Mai, an official of the Economic Committee; and Mr. Bourdvez and Mr. Okecki, sent by the League of Nations to our country, and many others. They all borrowed a small boat from the Public Security Bureau in advance and drove to the Huangpu River berth at six o'clock to welcome them.

Disembarkation Situation 120

The "Aramis" on which Mr. Coursin was traveling and the "Conte Verde" on which Mr. Omades was traveling were originally scheduled to arrive outside the Wusongkou the night before. Therefore, Guo Dehua and other welcoming personnel sent by the Economic Committee came to Shanghai from Beijing the day before to welcome them. Unexpectedly, the two ships encountered wind on the way, and arrived only yesterday morning. At 6:10 am and 7:10 am, the Italian and French ships were welcomed into the ship one after another, and then they sailed to the new customs wharf to disembark and went directly to the Cathay Hotel to rest.

Yesterday's Activities 121

After arriving at 7:30 yesterday morning, the two experts, Coursin and Omades, accompanied by Guo Dehua and others, took a car to the city center area to inspect the construction of Greater Shanghai and road projects in the morning, and returned at noon. At 2:00 pm, they went to the Shanghai office of the Economic Committee on Qizhi Road to visit Song Ziwen, a member of the Standing Committee, and inquired about the recent administrative facilities of the Economic Committee in detail. They left after a long time. At 7:30 in the evening, Guo Dehua hosted a welcome dinner at the Xinghualou Restaurant, and the guests and hosts dispersed happily at 8:30.

Background of the Two Gentlemen 122

Coursin, one of the two experts who came to China, is French and is over fifty years old. He was the Director of the Public Works Bureau of Madagascar, France, and has extensive experience in highway traffic. Omades is Italian and is still a world-famous water conservancy expert. He has served in the water conservancy agency in Italy for thirty or forty years and is over sixty years old this year. He is currently a reporter of the League of Nations Transportation and Public Works Committee and a consultant engineer in Milan.

Sincere Conversation 123

The Huadong News Agency reporter met the two gentlemen at the hotel last night and asked about the work situation after this trip to China. According to them, they were very pleased to come to Shanghai. China is a cultural country with a very long history in the world, so they very much wanted to take a long trip. They will inspect water conservancy, transportation, and construction work throughout China to seek improvements or other plans. They are willing to do their best to provide loyal service to China, as the Chinese serve China, etc.

Head to Hangzhou This Morning 124

After arriving in Shanghai yesterday, Mr. Coursin decided not to stay long because this trip to China will not last long. He has decided to leave Shanghai by car at 8:00 this morning, take the Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway to Hangzhou, take a brief tour of Hangzhou, inspect the construction situation in Zhejiang Province, and then go to Beijing to visit the members of our country's Economic Committee. The two experts will travel together first, and then separate when necessary. It can be completed by February 17 next spring, and then they will draft an investigation report and contribute a plan to our authorities for adoption. Also, Mr. Sartori, an assistant who came with Mr. Omades, is also a famous engineer.

Itinerary 125

The itinerary of the two experts will cover all parts of the country, from today to February 17 next year. Good, a member of the London Institution of Civil Engineers, and Nie Yufu, a reporter of the League of Nations Engineering Committee, have also started their journey to China. Good is expected to arrive on the 15th of this month, and Nie is expected to arrive in China at the end of this month. These two are also to investigate our country's water conservancy and transportation projects and promote the success of technical cooperation plans with our country.

Anti-Disaster Drill at the South Railway Station Yesterday Morning 127

Enemy Planes Attacking and Thugs Disturbing Were Not Successful

Employees Were Very Tired, Drill Suspended This Morning

In order to prevent disasters and protect railway traffic, the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration carried out prevention measures in the event of a major disaster on the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo lines respectively. Hangzhou, Jiaxing, and other stations have all completed the drills one after another. As a result, the performance evaluations were all good. Yesterday morning, the Shanghai South Railway Station conducted a major anti-disaster drill from 3:00 am to 4:00 am, lasting one hour. The most serious moment was the twenty minutes from 3:30 am to 3:50 am. At this time, the South Railway Station was in a state of extreme horror, as if a major disaster had struck. The details of the drill are recorded as follows:

Full Mobilization and Division of Responsibilities 128

At about 3:00 am yesterday morning, the Shanghai South Railway Station anti-disaster drill was held. Participants included all railway police officers of the Shanghai-Jiaxing Section of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Police Department, and all railway police officers and workers of the Engineering Section, Mechanical Section, and Health Section of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway. Zhong Wenjiang, the captain of the Shanghai-Jiaxing Section, served as the chief instructor, and Han Shangying, the deputy captain of the Shanghai-Jiaxing Section, Luo Shenghao, an engineer of the Engineering Section, Shi Ziyu, an engineer of the Mechanical Section, and Zheng Binshi, a doctor of the Health Section, served as deputy instructors. Zhou Binwu, the stationmaster, was in charge of train management, Liang Peigen, the director of the Locomotive Section, was in charge of lighting management, and Ma Xiaoping, the director of the Railway Police Department, and Li Jing, the director of the Ximen Public Security Bureau, and Yuan, the inspector of the Gaochang Temple Public Security Bureau, all came to visit.

Purpose of the Drill is to Prepare for Contingencies 129

When the Xinsheng News Agency reporter drove to the South Railway Station, the entire station was still peaceful as if nothing had happened. Han Shangying, the deputy captain of the Shanghai-Jiaxing Section, greeted reporters from various newspapers who participated in the disaster prevention news work and reported the significance of this railway administration's disaster prevention drill, so that if there were any omissions in the drill, they could be corrected and compensated in advance to avoid being caught unprepared in the event of a real disaster. The Xinsheng News Agency reporter then went to inspect the vicinity of the station. The South Railway Station in the middle of the night was silent. Only a thatched hut was pre-built behind the station for use as a burning target for aircraft bombing.

Alarms Ring Repeatedly, Suddenly Tense 130

At 3:00 am, the Shanghai-Jiaxing Section of the Railway Police stationed in the office had slight movements, and then the rescue team of the Health Section, the engineering team of the Engineering Section, the Mechanical Section, etc. of the South Railway Station also dispatched one after another. At 3:25 am, the alarm bell at the southern end of the station suddenly rang, indicating that the station authorities had received an alarm from Jiaxing, assuming that the enemy's enemy plane had advanced eastward to attack the Shanghai South Railway Station. At this time, the personnel dispatched were also suddenly tense. At 3:30 am, the second alarm bell rang again, meaning that the enemy plane had passed Jiaxing and was gradually approaching. Martial law was suddenly declared within half a mile of the station, and the railway police were all over the station, with overlapping police posts in important places. The fire brigade also crawled out to extinguish the fire. At 3:30 am, the third alarm bell rang urgently, as if the enemy's enemy plane was approaching even closer. All the lights in the station suddenly went out, and the whistles sounded one after another. The personnel participating in the disaster prevention issued an emergency mobilization order in the darkness. At this time, the South Railway Station had fallen into an extremely terrifying state.

Terror Arrives, Rescue is Rapid 131

At this time, the chief and deputy instructors at the station scattered with their teams, intending to assume that there were three enemy aircraft, two coming from the south and one from the east, dropping incendiary bombs near the station. Before long, the thatched house at the back door of the South Railway Station on the road in front of the station caught fire, and the flames soared into the sky for a while, almost causing a catastrophe. Fortunately, the railway police and fire brigade rushed to the scene and bravely rescued the fire with fire extinguishers, sandbags, and other fire-fighting equipment. It was extinguished in only a quarter of an hour, and other places were fortunately not burned. At this time, the aircraft bombings were even more intense, and the situation in the entire station was extremely chaotic. The injured were rushed to the temporary hospital by the rescue team with stretchers to take first aid medicine and treatment. The thugs also took advantage of the chaos to carry out sabotage. As a result, the tracks were destroyed and dismantled, two thugs were captured and tied up, and the locomotive for repairing the tracks was also driven out of the garage, carrying the engineering team and various track repair materials, and stopped at the destroyed place. The entire team started to repair the tracks. The speed of the engineering effect was unexpected. The train passed through the section of the tracks in only five minutes. At this time, another group of thugs rushed into the station to carry out sabotage, overturning objects and setting fires. Fortunately, the railway police were brave and alert and were able to capture all of them. The arrested thugs were reported to the chief instructor. Li Wenjin and Dai Shiguang, two thugs who destroyed the tracks, and Shi Wenbo and Zhang Shouqin, thugs who broke into the station and caused chaos, were captured. After interrogation, they were handed over to the custody.

Enemy Planes Fly Away, Order Restored 132

The enemy aircraft, failing to drop bombs, fled to the southwest. Thus, the scene of a major disaster came to an end, and the electric lights in the entire station were as bright as ever, and order and traffic gradually returned. The Xinsheng News Agency reporter met with the chief instructor Zhong Wenhong at the station again, saying that the exercise tonight had achieved unexpected results, so the two exercises this morning and tomorrow will not be held again.

Work Fatigue, Continued Exercise Suspended 133

The Xinsheng News Agency reporter learned from the Railway Administration yesterday morning that the Shanghai South Railway Station conducted an air defense drill yesterday morning and originally planned to hold it officially this morning. However, the results of the test run were very good, and all the staff were very tired after working hard. Moreover, the Railway Administration has been very busy with various tasks recently, so it was decided to suspend the exercise. It is rumored that the Shanghai North Railway Station will hold a regular air defense drill, but it has also been decided to abandon it.

Today's Commemoration of the Zhaohe Uprising 143

Held at the City Party Headquarters at 10:00 AM

Today marks the 19th anniversary of the Zhaohe warship uprising. All sectors of the city's populace have scheduled a commemorative meeting for 10:00 AM today at the Grand Auditorium of the City Party Headquarters in Fenglin Bridge. The City Party Headquarters yesterday issued a special notice to all city agencies, schools, and organizations, requesting them to send two representatives each, with letters of participation. Standing Committee Member Tong Xingbai has been designated chairman. At the same time, Yang Hu, then Chief of the City Security Department who participated in the uprising, has been invited to attend and report on the situation at the time. The Chinese Concession military and police agencies, in addition to strictly implementing winter defense measures and maintaining security, have added extra protection. The City Party Headquarters, to ensure that all sectors understand the significance of the uprising, has also issued a public notice, which states:

The Zhaohe Warship and Mr. Yang Xiaotian at the Time of the Uprising

The image shows Yang Hu, acting Naval Commander in 1915 during the Zhaohe Incident, leading troops to occupy the warship. After occupying the ship, he raised the party flag at the masthead and gave a speech. The left corner shows a recent photo of Mr. Yang.

Today is the anniversary of the Zhaohe Uprising. The Special Party Headquarters of the City Security Department considers this event to be the herald of the campaign to overthrow Yuan Shikai and protect the nation, and the precursor to the rebuilding of the Republic. Furthermore, Mr. Yang Xiaotian, the Standing Committee Member of the association and Chief of the City Security Department, was the commander who led party members to seize the Zhaohe warship on that day. The tragic and ardent events certainly have much to tell. Therefore, at 10:00 AM today, representatives of the teams will be gathered for a commemorative ceremony, and Mr. Yang will be invited to attend and report on the uprising to invigorate the revolutionary spirit and achieve the practical effect of saving the nation. According to Mr. Yang Xiaotian, Chief of the City Security Department, who personally participated in the Zhaohe Uprising, the Zhaohe Incident has passed many years. Thinking back, the impression is profoundly deep. He is specially publishing commemorative remarks to record his long-held sentiments. The record of his commemorative remarks is as follows:

Today is the nineteenth anniversary of the Zhaohe warship uprising. I have the honor of being one of the participants in the uprising and battle. As this important anniversary approaches, all compatriots and comrades across the country who are concerned about this history of the uprising may hope for my personal account. However, the details of the Zhaohe commemoration have been briefly recorded in party history and scattered in newspapers. Moreover, there has been narration every time we have held a commemoration. Therefore, I do not wish to add much more. What I will discuss today will focus on three aspects: the motives, effects, and evolving significance of the Zhaohe Uprising. ㈠ Motives: The general view of the motives for the Zhaohe Uprising is that it was a struggle by our party against Yuan Shikai's imperial ambitions and in support of democratic politics. This is, of course, a factual account of the matter. However, I would like to add that the overthrow of the empire and the support for democracy are merely the immediate causes that constitute this historical fact. There is an even longer historical development relationship at play. Since the philosopher Bacon advocated scientific practice in Europe, the social way of life has changed drastically from the past. England was the first to bear the brunt of this change, forming the famous industrial revolution in history. As a result, the surge in the economy influenced the organization of its political system. This is known to all who study world cultural history. It is consistent with what the historian Wells said in his European history regarding the evolution of monarchy and republic: [Political changes and intellectual development both increased, and are subtly related to science. Mankind has a growing tendency to want to consider life based on common fundamental desires and unsatisfied enjoyments, and to explore the relationships of life in a broader sense, serving and enjoying.] This is one aspect. At the same time, as the wheel of the era advanced into the twentieth century, industry in Europe and the United States had developed to a dangerous point where it was necessary to invade others. In fact, other industrially backward countries in the world, such as Africa and Asia, immediately became the grazing grounds for industrialized nations. They plundered and seized to the extreme. Moreover, the biologist Darwin advocated the dangerous theories of [survival of the fittest and the strong preying on the weak]. The world was in turmoil, and there was no end in sight. This is the second aspect. On the other hand, although we have had thousands of years of emperors, historical records still record the public ownership of the world by Yao and Shun, the utopian society of the Lao and Mo schools, and the Confucian political theories of [the people are the most important] and [the virtuous should rule]. Our people live in this kind of historical culture, which will naturally evolve into an unknown political system in the future. This is the third aspect. Furthermore, in the West, there is the practical experiment of the French republican political system, the democratic governance of the United States in the New World, and the constitutionalism of England, Germany, Italy, Japan, and other countries. All of these are the beginnings of democracy. This is the fourth aspect. These four causes together constitute the Three Principles of the People—nationalism, democracy, and people's livelihood—the doctrine of national salvation of the late Premier. Therefore, our party must eliminate all those who oppose or contradict this doctrine as opportunities arise. Therefore, Yuan Shikai's imperial ambitions are naturally not to be tolerated. To put it bluntly, it is our party's late Premier using his Three Principles of the People to eliminate those reactionary factions who have already formed. Therefore, I state that the Zhaohe Uprising, in addition to eliminating the already established traitors, also contains a distant historical development. ㈡ Effects: Those who discuss the history of our party's revolution have often considered the Zhaohe Uprising to be the preface to the rebuilding of the Republic, with the Yunnan Uprising as the rearguard. Some even believe that the Zhaohe Uprising was the prelude to the success of the Northern Expedition and the unification of the country by our party. In my opinion, the above points are only inferences based on the evolution of the revolutionary battles. To be realistic, the victory of revolutionary theory is still important. The victory of military force is only temporary, deformed, and not a true victory. This is not only true today, but is also clearly revealed in ancient history, both Chinese and foreign. If the revolution relied entirely on military force, then our party's initial strength was like a drop in the ocean. To use it to fight against the Qing Dynasty was like a mantis trying to stop a cart. However, the reason why we were able to overthrow the Qing Dynasty in the end was that revolutionary theory prevailed. Furthermore, the Zhaohe Uprising not only dealt a fatal blow to domestic

reactionaries, but also contained the meaning of international resistance. When the traitor Yuan Shikai was self-respecting, he knew that he was offending the public, so he signed the Twenty-One Demands, which would destroy the country, by means of treason. The late Premier led our party comrades to call out, and the revolutionary tide of Huangpu rose. The traitor Yuan Shikai, who sold the country and harmed the people, died in shame because of this, and the Twenty-One Demands were shattered in their legal effect by the sound of the Zhaohe cannons. This is why I say that the effect of the Zhaohe Uprising, in addition to what is generally recognized, also carries the international rejection of war and the victory of revolutionary theory. ㈢ Evolving Significance: The significance of revolution contains two principles: destruction and construction. Destruction is certainly not easy, but construction is even more difficult. The late Premier has explained these fundamental principles to our compatriots and comrades in detail. Today, as we commemorate the Zhaohe Uprising, we are truly admiring the bloodshed and destruction of the martyrs. The path was difficult, and cutting through the thorns was not easy. This is certainly essential. However, as time passes and years change, it is not enough to only admire or imitate the destructive spirit of the martyrs. Now that the government is unified and the military period is over, there are many things to be done. In this solemn commemoration of the martyrs, our compatriots and comrades should, based on the sages who sacrificed their lives for righteousness, strive for the grand plan of building a hundred things. This is the evolution of the meaning of revolution. The lost territory in the Northeast has not been recovered, the Naval Conference has collapsed, and the disarmament conference is even more of a castle in the air. The economic downturn and the people's hardship are unprecedented in human history. I deeply hope that my compatriots and comrades will have great insight and, under the leadership of the central government, work hard and prepare to be martyrs who defend the nation and uphold the doctrine, so that we will be worthy of our lives. The righteous act of the Zhaohe Uprising, which the late Premier commanded on this day nineteen years ago, will coexist with heaven and earth. Although I am not talented, I am willing to encourage us together.

Two More Ships of the Sanbei Company Encountered Danger 148

But Both Were Safe

Waking Lion Aground The Waking Lion ship of the Sanbei Company originally sailed the Yangtze River. Recently, due to the large number of ships on the Yangtze River, it went to Haizhou to load salt. This time, it was transporting a large amount of salt from Shierxu to Hankou. Now is the winter season, and the Yangtze River is receding, making navigation difficult. The ship, at 1:00 AM yesterday morning, while approaching Datong, ran aground due to fog and the pilot's negligence. It was fully loaded with salt, and the draft was deep, causing the ship to sink into the shallows and unable to escape for a time. Yesterday, the company received the news and telegraphed all of its upriver and downriver ships on the Yangtze River to assist in towing it when passing by. The hull of the Waking Lion was not damaged. Once the tide rises, it is hoped that it can get out of the shallows.

Dragon Mountain Encountered Wind The Dragon Mountain ship of the Sanbei Company was going from Shanghai to Qinhuangdao to load coal. However, there was a hurricane in the sea area in recent days. The ship encountered a hurricane attack at around the morning yesterday when it was near Sheshan. At that time, the ship owner telegraphed for help and was assisted by a Chinese Navy warship. When reporters inquired, the person in charge of the company said that the Dragon Mountain encountering wind was not very dangerous. After the wind passes, it is hoped that it can sail again. The hull was not grounded on rocks.

After the Taishan Ship Accident 149

The crew members' families are demanding compensation

After the Sanbei Company's Taishan ship accident was confirmed, there were a total of 51 employees on board who were killed. The British Consulate in this port yesterday received a telegram from a British warship stating that two more bodies had been recovered, and that the rest were feared to be submerged inside the ship, unable to float to the surface for the time being. The families of the deceased employees went to the company yesterday to demand compensation, and the situation was very tragic.

Truth About the Disaster 150

The Taishan ship set sail from Qingdao at 7:00 AM on the 27th of last month, loaded with 3,050 tons of coal, plus coal for the ship's own use. The load had reached the safety line, and the ship's draft was too deep, reducing the hull's buoyancy. It would have been very dangerous even without wind and waves. The ship encountered a hurricane about 14 hours into the sea voyage from Qingdao. At that time, the China Merchants Bureau's Yongji ship was sailing ahead and also encountered a hurricane. The shipmaster of the Yongji quickly reduced the speed of his ship and sailed with the wind and waves. As a result, it was able to get out of the wind circle and fortunately escaped. The ship following behind was the Taishan, but it was already dark and the ship name could not be seen. The shipmaster of the Yongji saw that the ship suddenly turned its bow when the hurricane struck. The crew knew that the ship must have had an accident, but they saw the ship send out a distress signal. The Yongji itself had not yet escaped the wind circle and could not go to rescue it. They watched the ship sink, but they did not know its name at the time and could not determine which ship it was. It was not until the Yongji arrived in Shanghai and inquired whether any ships from various companies had not arrived that they learned that the ship that encountered the accident that the Yongji encountered was the Taishan.

Families Requesting Compensation 151

Yesterday morning, the families of the ship's crew, sailors, stokers, etc., went to the Sanbei Company on Guangdong Road, supporting the old and carrying the young. They were all wailing and crying loudly, demanding that the company pay compensation. The manager of the company comforted them one by one. Since the crew members were killed, there are regulations in the maritime law. After the company receives an official and confirmed report of the accident, it will be handled according to law. Moreover, the various shipping companies have established precedents for compensating the crew members who died, so the families should not be disappointed. Until 12:00 noon, the crew members' families left in tears.

Union Negotiations 152

The China Association of Marine Engineers sent a letter to the Sanbei Company yesterday, stating: "Dear Sirs, We have learned that your company's Taishan ship, which was on its way from Qingdao to Shanghai, has been missing for many days. According to reports, the British warship HMS Peterel has recovered four bodies 140 miles from Qingdao while sailing from Weihaiwei to Shanghai, all of which were carrying Taishan ship lifebuoys. Based on this situation, it is certain that the ship has been wrecked. The families of the crew members who served on the ship, upon hearing this news, have been gathering at our association day and night, supporting the old and carrying the young, crying out to heaven and earth, asking us to uphold justice and requesting that we send personnel to lead them to your company to negotiate in person. The tragic situation is unbearable to describe. According to our information, on the 26th of this month, in addition to the Taishan, your company also had the Shengan ship sailing from Qingdao to Shanghai. Although it set sail three hours before the Taishan, the actual speed of the Shengan was inferior to the Taishan. Why did one arrive safely in Shanghai, while the other encountered a strange accident midway? This is worth investigating. We urge your company to thoroughly investigate to clarify the truth and avoid any ambiguity. As for the aftermath, the most important point at present is that you should quickly send a ship to search along the route and salvage the bodies, including those recovered by the British warship, and transport them to Shanghai together for identification. You should also prepare coffins and provide generous burials to comfort the deceased. As for the issue of compensation, as your company is a giant in the shipping industry, you should be extra generous to ensure that the families of the deceased can live in peace and avoid the risk of freezing and starvation. We hope that your company will respond quickly upon receipt of this letter to avoid the families waiting for a long time and any unexpected events occurring, which would be inconvenient. We are sending this letter to inform you and ask you to investigate."
