The Zhejiang Public Bonds Mortgage Loan Contract Was Signed Yesterday 160

The borrowing banks will remit the full amount before the end of the month

The banking syndicate is organized with China Communications as its representative

The New Voice Society reported that the Zhejiang Provincial Government mortgaged 5 million yuan face value of local public bonds to China and other banks for 3 million yuan. After the contract was negotiated and finalized, it was sent to the banks for signing. The signing was completed yesterday, and it was decided that the full amount would be remitted once before the end of this month. The details are as follows:

Apportioned to Each Bank Zhejiang public bonds with a face value of 5 million yuan are mortgaged to banks at 60% for a loan of 3 million yuan. The borrowing banks are China, Communications, Shanghai, Zhejiang Industrial, Zhejiang Xingye, Zhejiang Local, Jincheng, Zhongnan, Continental, Yanye, Tongshang, Kenye, Siming, Agricultural and Industrial, China Industrial, China National Products, and other banks, as well as the Four-Bank Savings Association, totaling 20. The borrowing banks have also organized a banking syndicate and entrusted China and Communications Banks as representatives of the syndicate.

Signing Completed After the loan contract was negotiated, there were a total of two copies, one for the Zhejiang Provincial Government and one for the borrowing banks' syndicate. After being finalized, Wang Chengying, Director of the Zhejiang Department of Finance, carried them to Hangzhou. After being passed by the Provincial Government meeting, the signing began in Hangzhou. All borrowing banks that have a head office or branch in Hangzhou signed in Hangzhou. If there is no branch in Hangzhou, Xu Enpei, General Manager of Zhejiang Local Bank, carried them to Shanghai again a few days ago and handed them over to banks without a branch in Hangzhou, such as Shanghai, Siming, Kenye, and National Products, for signing. The signing was completed yesterday.

Remitted in One Lump Sum Each borrowing bank will keep one copy of the signed contract for reference. The total amount of 3 million yuan, the monthly interest is 8%, and the term is two years. The stipulated use is as follows: 1 million yuan will be used to handle emergency disaster relief for the drought in various parts of Zhejiang, and 2 million yuan will be used to cover the previous administrative expenses of Zhejiang Province. It is stipulated that before the end of this month, all borrowing banks will remit the amount borrowed at one time to China and Communications Banks in Hangzhou, which will then be transferred to the Zhejiang Department of Finance. At the same time, the Department of Finance will hand over the public bonds with a face value of 5 million yuan to China and Communications Banks in Hangzhou, which will then be distributed to the banks in proportion to the amount borrowed.

Special Report

International Situation and China's Way Out by Li Fusun 161

Mr. Li Fusun, a leader in the financial world, traveled abroad to Europe and America for inspection during the summer of this year. After returning to China, various groups and newspaper reporters successively requested lectures and the publication of his opinions. Mr. Li, due to the complexity of his affairs, was unable to respond to each invitation individually. Therefore, he entrusted the publication of the following document to satisfy the earnest expectations of all parties and to spare those who wished to hear Mr. Li's views the labor of traveling. This will, no doubt, be welcomed by readers.

International conflicts, after the relief and discharge of the last World War, had temporarily returned to peace and harmony, and in their place, various international cooperative movements arose. However, before long, the world economic panic occurred, which has lasted for five years from 1929 to the present. The advance of the panic has not diminished in the slightest. In the process of the panic, countries have sought their own salvation. On the one hand, they have built high tariff barriers to prevent the intrusion of foreign goods, and on the other hand, they have reduced the value of their currencies to seize overseas markets. As economic warfare has intensified, the momentum of nationalism has risen, and the so-called international cooperation has once again become a bubble. The failure of past disarmament conferences, the futility of world economic conferences, and the current stalemate of the naval disarmament preparatory conference are all extremely obvious facts.

Markets are limited, but the development of productivity is advancing day by day. If advanced countries only possess domestic markets, they are insufficient to absorb their huge productivity, and to seize overseas markets is nothing more than treating neighbors as cesspools. The countries seek to retaliate against each other, which only makes the markets narrower and sales more sluggish. Using this to overcome the panic, it is no wonder that the panic remains, and international conflicts grow daily, with even the worry of a re-enactment of a world war.

Looking at the economic conditions of European and American countries, the relatively stable one is Great Britain. British industry and commerce have a long history and a solid foundation, and the extent of its colonies far exceeds other countries. Since the Ottawa Conference, the subordinate countries within the British Empire have further established close ties to prevent the outflow of rights and interests. British colonial policy has always emphasized tolerance, and other countries could still get a piece of the pie in colonial trade. However, in recent years, due to the urgency of self-preservation, it has become necessary to gradually squeeze out the influence of other countries outside the British Empire. It is precisely because of this change in policy that Great Britain has been able to compensate for a portion of the losses in foreign trade by increasing trade with its colonies and domestic trade, thereby alleviating its internal panic. Its sound financial system is sufficient to calm people's hearts and influence national policy, enabling the entire country, from top to bottom, to calmly deal with the turbulent waves with a gentle and steady policy, achieving results that others cannot match.

Among the British industrial sectors, the most unfortunate is the textile industry. The desolation in the Lancashire area remains unchanged. This is because the textile industry is one of the light industries, easily imitated by latecomer countries and colonies. The development of the textile industries in China and India is a crisis for the British textile industry, but its fatal wound is the rapid advancement of Japanese textile technology and its low wages. When we observe the impact of Japanese-owned yarn factories on Chinese-owned yarn factories, we can see what kind of impact the high wages in Britain have suffered.

In these difficult times, how should we conduct ourselves? When nationalism is rampant, hoping to assist China's development through international cooperation is probably a futile dream. Since the September 18th Incident, the balance of power in the Far East has been broken, and international cooperation schemes are plagued by many difficulties and considerations, which may not be allowed by the situation. If we want to fight for the survival of the nation, we can only rely on self-reliance and self-rescue. Under the principle of self-reliance and self-rescue, we must especially weigh the priorities and carefully consider the gains and losses. The law should indeed take the strengths of others to supplement our weaknesses, and the application must rely on what we uniquely possess and adapt to what we urgently need. In all measures, we must strive to minimize harms and maximize benefits, and achieve great effects with little effort. Only by exerting all our efforts will we see results. Based on this meaning, there is no doubt that the foundation of the nation should be based on agriculture. The reason why our country has been less affected by the world panic in the past five years is that the maintenance of the silver standard, which has brought us the benefits of collecting revenue, is one of the reasons, but establishing the country on agriculture, with the economic foundation spread in the countryside rather than concentrated in the cities, has prevented the panic's tidal wave from finding its focus of attack, which is a powerful defense. European countries such as Denmark have also experienced less panic for this reason. While the countryside is more resistant to panic, it still relies on the support of national policy to avoid ultimate exhaustion. In recent years, in addition to man-made disasters, natural disasters have increased in our country, and the rural economy has gradually fallen into hardship. Even the annual import of agricultural products, reaching 400 to 500 million yuan, is alarming. Given our country's abundant natural resources, improving agricultural production to achieve self-sufficiency should not be difficult. If this is the case, the most serious trade deficit and financial problems in the national economy can be easily solved, which will not only preserve the existing rural foundation.

Under the policy of emphasizing agriculture, the transportation industry must seek its development. Otherwise, even if production increases, the surplus and deficit will not be balanced, which would be in vain. However, the construction of transportation tools must not go against the policy of emphasizing agriculture. The fundraising for construction expenses must not harm the vitality of the countryside, and the function of transportation tools should be able to undertake the important task of dredging agricultural products. Following these measures, minerals can also be developed along with agricultural products. By taking advantage of the benefits of nature and exhausting the efforts of people, the establishment of the national foundation can be achieved with half the effort and twice the result.

As for industry, existing factories should be vigorously supported and encouraged in various ways. For new industries that are still in the planning stage or require large amounts of capital, it seems better to establish appropriate procedures to welcome the cooperation of foreign capital. Being greedy for more and seeking quick results, and being fond of grand achievements are the biggest weaknesses of our people. For decades, we have only possessed the empty name of maintaining rights and have not received the actual benefits of developing rights and interests. Hiding treasures only teaches thieves, which is disheartening. Based on the above situation, it is feared that even if we gather the manpower and financial resources of the whole country to revitalize the countryside and develop natural resources, the results may still be insufficient. After revitalizing the countryside and developing natural resources, the national foundation will be established, and there will be no need to seek external solutions. If we abandon the near and pursue the far, and divert limited manpower and financial resources to industry, the protection of tariffs will be difficult to ensure, and the improvement of technology cannot be achieved overnight. After the bankruptcy of the countryside, sales will become a problem. Its foundation is so fragile, and to compete with others for a moment's advantage is like hitting a stone with an egg. I fear that we will be stretched on all sides, losing sight of one thing while attending to another, and that both industry and agriculture will fall into ruin. Therefore, I hope that the whole country, from top to bottom, will break free from prejudices, be practical and realistic, and use the limited national power in the most cautious and economical way. The first step is to ensure that the three main agricultural products, rice, wheat, and cotton, are sufficient to meet our needs for food and clothing. The second step is to export what is left over to reduce the trade deficit. If we can do this, the rural economy and its purchasing power will naturally recover, and the exhaustion of inland finance and the depression of cities will naturally disappear. Then, we can use the recovered financial resources to engage in industry, which will be easier and smoother. In short, it is not that I do not consider industry important, but since we cannot take care of everything, it is better to prioritize what is urgent. Here, it is necessary to emphasize that hoping for international cooperation to develop China is one thing, and welcoming foreign capital to cooperate in developing industry is another. Any joint plan among international parties is impossible, while private investment by capitalists from various countries in the nature of simple business investment is very possible. However, in this situation, the principle of self-reliance and self-rescue must still be fully realized. The entire financial industry in the country should unite and organize a sound organization to directly negotiate with financiers and entrepreneurs from various countries, providing them with sufficient assistance and communication. Only when we have a sound organization and strength ourselves, will foreign capitalists be pleased to come to us after hearing about it. We must thoroughly recognize that the investment of foreign capitalists is purely voluntary. If the investment is safe and profitable, they will come without being invited, and it is up to us to make good use of it. If we want to attract huge sums of money based solely on the tongues of one or two lobbyists, I fear that the result will be the opposite.

As for the currency system, the people's understanding of currency is still very immature. The hard currency centrism of the metallist school is still a timely theory in our country. The laws of using artificial methods and political means to control currency, which can barely achieve temporary effects in other countries, have little possibility of being imitated in our country. The recent scheme adopted by our country to impose an active tariff on silver exports is a practical and effective law. As a result, it only makes silver depreciate in international exchange, which is sufficient to prevent the massive export of currency materials and maintain the stability of prices domestically, without any impact on the currency itself, and the foundation of the currency system is firmly unshaken. Here, I hope that domestic scholars will deeply study the domestic situation and national environment, and avoid sensationalist theories to shake people's hearts and cause unnecessary panic. The market will be safe.

Finally, I have an incidental statement to make. My trip abroad was purely a private tour. I am grateful to the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for their letters of introduction, which provided many conveniences on the journey. However, I did not assume any formal mission at the beginning. Although the Ministry of Finance instructed me to investigate the currency systems of various countries along the way, at a time when the currency systems of various countries are divorced from the economic field and transferred to political management, what I have seen is only a myriad of laws and regulations, and there are few natural laws of currency that can be imitated, and even fewer that can be studied.

Page 11

Police File Lawsuit Against Liang Tongfang Case Opened Yesterday 162

Liang said that because there were few customers at noon, he went to warn them

If he had the determination to kill, why would he bother to explain?

Liang Tongfang from Shangyu, because he took a bomb to Yuelai South Goods Store on Guangdong Road to warn them not to sell enemy goods, the bomb fell on the counter, causing an explosion. In addition to blowing off Liang's right wrist and two fingers of his left hand, three employees and one customer in the store were slightly injured. Liang was arrested on the spot by the police and sent to the hospital with the injured for treatment. The Public Concession then filed a public lawsuit against Liang for attempted murder under Article 284 of the Criminal Law. After investigation by the First Special District Court, it was determined that Liang had no intention of premeditated murder and was convicted of possessing explosives with intent to commit a crime under Article 200 of the Criminal Law, sentenced to six months imprisonment, and suspended for two years. After Liang was sentenced, the Shangyu Association in Shanghai and others tried to bail him out from the court and sent him to the hospital for treatment. However, the Public Concession was very dissatisfied with the first instance judgment, and the lawyer in charge, Wang Yaotang, filed an appeal with the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court.

File Appeal 163

The reasons stated in the appeal were very detailed, generally stating that after Liang Tongfang joined the "Red Exterminating Traitors Group" in Shanghai, he distributed leaflets and sent warning letters to commercial firms rumored to be selling Japanese goods, threatening them with death if they did not comply. According to his confession, he also gave the same warning to Yuelai South Goods Store, and a letter was also sent at the same time. When the police officers went to the defendant's residence to search, they did indeed find the leaflet, indicating that his motive for murder had been established since he joined the illegal organization. Later, because he believed that the warning to Yuelai was ineffective, he gathered his comrades and discussed together in a closed room in the Heming Hotel on how to implement the final step, which was also confessed. After the discussion was settled, at noon on October 19th, he took a very powerful bomb to Yuelai to carry out the murder. After the defendant spoke three or two words with the store employee,

Immediately Throw Bomb 164

Causing injury to the store employee and customers. According to the murder charge, intent is a necessary condition, which is clearly stipulated by the law. However, the word "intent" has a certain definition. Article 26 of the Criminal Law stipulates [“Whoever clearly knows the facts constituting the crime and intentionally causes it to occur is intentional.”] Now, the bomb thrown by the defendant is an immediate explosive. Once thrown, its power is great enough to kill many people at the same time, as is known to ordinary people. How could the defendant, who was a soldier and experienced war, not know? Even his confession in the first instance stated that the bomb would explode immediately. Therefore, the defendant knew that the bomb he used was a weapon for murder, which is beyond doubt. According to the defendant's confession, he had removed the safety pin before throwing it, indicating that his determination to kill was consistent from the beginning. Who would believe that he did not intend to kill? Therefore, he was a premeditated murderer, which is beyond doubt. Furthermore, after the defendant was sentenced in the first instance, he published an advertisement in the Shanghai Evening News on November 24th to thank all sectors, which contained

The Phrase "Corpse Admonition" 165

Although the original meaning of the phrase "corpse admonition" is to use one's dead body to go to someone else's place to admonish, the circumstances of this case are different from perishing together with others. However, his determination to die can be seen in general. The original judgment tried hard to exonerate the defendant. The reasons for proving that the defendant did not have premeditated murder were: 1) The defendant intended to warn before throwing the bomb; 2) He did not throw the bomb, but slipped; 3) The method of throwing was not enough to cause the death of others. It only knew one thing and did not know the other. The original lawsuit for attempted murder was true and well-founded, and there was no flaw to attack. The original judgment did not impose the appropriate punishment according to the indictment, but avoided the heavier and chose the lighter, and changed the conviction to possession of explosives, sentencing him to six months in prison and then suspending it. In terms of law, there is no justification, and according to past precedents,

Cases Of Same Nature 166

There are those who have been sentenced to twelve years in prison, which is extremely inconsistent with previous examples. Even if the circumstances of the defendant's crime have something to be pitied, one should not distort the law and erase the facts. To allow the people to indulge in their impulses, disregard the law, or even consider it profitable, is a phenomenon that should not exist in a rule-of-law country. Therefore, I request that the original judgment be revoked and that the defendant be punished with the punishment he deserves, etc. Yesterday afternoon, Zhao, Wu, and Zhou, the three judges of the High Court's Second Branch, specially opened a collegial panel to hear the case. Prosecutor Zhong Qing also attended the court to perform his duties. First, Judge Zhao asked Liang Tongfang about his name, origin, age, and residence. Then, Wang Yaotang, the lawyer representing the Public Concession, stated the intention of the appeal, stating that the Public Concession believed that the first-instance judgment of November 17th was wrong. All the reasons for the appeal have been stated in detail in the statement of reasons. Please

Revoke Original Judgement 167

And convict him of attempted premeditated murder in accordance with Article 2824 of the original lawsuit, and submit the Social Evening News, which contains Liang Tongfang's advertisement of thanks to all sectors, as evidence. Judge Zhao then questioned the appellant Liang Tongfang, who stated that he had heard the appeal intention stated by the Public Concession's lawyer, but he had no intention of intentionally injuring anyone. The discussion with his comrades in the Heming Hotel beforehand was also to discuss how to avoid injury, and there was no premeditation on how to injure anyone. Therefore, he decided to go to warn them at noon, because it was lunchtime and there would be few customers. He had sent two letters to Yuelai in advance to warn them, advising them not to sell enemy goods again during this economic panic, which would benefit the enemy. However, the store did not listen, so he took the bomb and went to the store alone to warn them again. Because the store employee did not understand my language, he showed the newspaper with the bomb, and told the colleagues in the store to leave quickly. Unexpectedly, at this moment,

The bomb in his hand 168

Suddenly fell on the counter, causing an explosion. If I had premeditated murder, I would have thrown the bomb inside as soon as I entered the store, so why would I bother to speak? And I would not have suffered the misfortune myself. The court then questioned him about the advertisement he posted, saying that there were words in the advertisement such as "unable to commit suicide in the store," which seemed to imply perishing together. Liang immediately replied that the advertisement was posted by the fellow villagers' association, and after I saw it, I posted another advertisement to correct it, so the wording was not my intention, etc. The court determined that the facts of the case had been investigated and clarified, and ordered the debate to begin. The Public Concession's lawyer spoke first, stating that since all the reasons had been explained in detail, he would only use a few words to request that the errors that the Public Concession believed to be in the first-instance judgment be corrected, and that the defendant be convicted of attempted premeditated murder. Then, Ge Zhaoji, Feng Meixue, Feng Buqing, and other three lawyers hired by the Shangyu fellow villagers' association to defend Liang

Sequentially Defended 169

Stating that the original judgment was very fair. Although the police still requested that he be punished for attempted premeditated murder, the defendant has now confessed in detail the cause of the bomb explosion, which is sufficient to prove that he did go to warn them at that time and had no intention of hurting anyone. Unfortunately, he lost his hand and fell. Although he had injured people, Liang himself was the most seriously injured. His motive for committing the crime was purely a patriotic heart, aroused by righteous indignation. Therefore, he was willing to sacrifice himself in the hope of awakening the traitors and making them aware. The highest principle of the country's creation of laws and punishing criminals is to make the offenders change their ways and do good, and not to fall into the criminal law again. The defendant is now disabled, and he is actually unable to continue to commit illegal acts. From now on, he will have the heart to love the country, but he will not be able to work. I would like to ask the presiding judge to forgive the circumstances and still maintain the original judgment and reject the Public Concession's appeal. After the debate was over, Judge Zhao announced that the sentence would be announced on the afternoon of the 11th of this month, and Liang Tongfang was still allowed to be released on the original bail.

Various yarn factories oppose the increase of the unified tax and send representatives to Beijing to petition again 170

Guo Shun and four others will depart tonight

Since the national Chinese yarn factories learned that the Ministry of Finance intended to levy a unified tax on cotton yarn, they convened an emergency representative meeting of national yarn industry leaders to discuss countermeasures. They all believed that the yarn industry was already difficult to maintain under the pressure, how could it bear additional burdens? It was resolved to send representatives to Beijing to petition the relevant ministries and departments to cancel this proposal. The government authorities agreed to submit it to the Central Political Council for review and amendment. So far, there has been no reply. The yarn factories have become increasingly anxious, and at the previous regular meeting of the Yarn Association, they raised the issue for discussion again and decided to send representatives Guo Shun, Nie Lusheng, Liu Jingji, Zhang Zemin, etc. to Beijing to petition again to achieve the goal of cancellation. If it is unsuccessful, they plan to petition at the Fifth Plenary Session of the Central Committee so that the future of the yarn industry will not be in a situation of being "kicked when it's down". The above representatives are scheduled to take the Beijing-Shanghai night express train to Beijing at 11:00 tonight (5th).

The United States Needs Hair Brushes, Flannel Pajamas

Germany Needs Raw Materials Such As Wool, Camel Hair

According to the International Trade Bureau yesterday, the German Aiwarte Baolai Company needs raw wool and camel hair, and the American Southern Import Company needs daily necessities. The following is a record of the goods needed. The northwestern provinces of our country are rich in wool. Every year, it is transported from the Ping-Sui Railway to Tianjin, and after being sorted and cleaned, it is exported to European and American countries, and the number is quite large. According to the statistics of 1933, the output of goat hair was 15,807 piculs, worth 1,599,032 taels of silver, sheep wool was 225,261 piculs, worth 11,522,891 taels of silver, and camel hair was 15,279 piculs, worth 1,827,103 taels of silver, accounting for a considerable position in foreign trade. The wool produced in our country has slightly coarser fibers than that produced in Australia, and can be used to weave inferior wool fabrics, blankets, felts, etc. Now, the German Liupse City Aiwarte Baolai Company has sent a letter requesting Peruvian wool, Angora goat hair, camel hair, and waste wool left over after combing machines have worked. It has sent a letter to purchase jewelry boxes, hairbrushes, toothbrushes, socks, flannel pants and pajamas, etc. If each manufacturer wishes to sell to the country, they can send a letter to the Bureau for introduction.

<Purpose of the Survey P]　　During the past month, I (referring to myself, Jing Jun) have visited important cities in the five provinces of Hebei, Shandong, Shaanxi, Hubei, and Hunan, such as Beiping, Tianjin, Xi'an, Hankou, Changsha, Xuzhou, and other places. The purpose of this survey was to determine, amid the current economic downturn, whether there is a chance for the revival of Chinese national products. In each place I visited, I made sure to first inquire in detail about the situation from important local industrialists and merchants. I then visited local factories, construction sites, transportation facilities, municipal works, and researched various aspects related to national products. Therefore, although this trip was short, I gained a lot and am willing to share what I know with my fellow advocates of national products as a relevant reference. 174

A Promising Future

The position of national products in North China has already seen significant development. Various general industries and small factories are gradually flourishing. People's practical skills are also progressing compared to the past. This is due to the combined efforts of all parties. Take cigarettes as an example: in the past, they were entirely under the influence of foreign merchants, but that is no longer the case. For example, our company's Ginseng brand is now enjoyed by the public and will soon form a competitive position against imported goods. The same can be said for other products. Xi'an has been identified by the national products industry and the banking sector as the central point for developing the Northwest. Future development is not far off. The Central China market is also optimistic. All parties have a deep understanding of national products. Even before the original economic strength has fully recovered, the important hub of the Yangtze River basin is still firmly held due to the joint efforts of the government and the people to seek prosperity. In summary, there are three impressions gained from this trip: (1) the government authorities are quite serious about promoting national products, (2) they are willing to support them with real strength, and (3) the people are mostly able to support national products. In addition, if the national products industry can put more effort into research in manufacturing and consider the psychology of consumers, then the day of the revival of national products is at hand.

Jin Ai-ru Stole Important Items from Safe Deposit Box

Transferred from Shanghai Bank to Zhejiang Industrial Bank

Account Name Unchanged, Discovery Due to Change Notification

Hu Dunyi, courtesy name Boyi, a consultant to the Jiangxi Provincial Relief Committee and a standing committee member of the Jiangxi Charity Federation, previously stored gold jewelry and other items worth over ten thousand yuan in safe deposit box number 3394 at the Shanghai Bank. Recently, Hu came to Shanghai with his nephew, Jin Ai-ru. Unexpectedly, Jin stole the keys and seals to Hu's safe deposit box and secretly opened the box at the Shanghai Bank, taking out all the items and transferring them to safe deposit box number 401 at the Zhejiang Industrial Bank. The account name remained Hu Boyi, but the address was written as his original residence at 47 Land Temple, Jiangxi. Recently, the new building of the Zhejiang Industrial Bank was completed, and the entire bank moved into the new premises. The head office notified all safe deposit box holders to change to new boxes before December 10. Jin was also notified. Although the location was Jin's residence, the account name was still Hu Boyi. The postal workers, knowing Hu's address, saw that the address and name did not match and assumed that the sender had written the address incorrectly. They sent the notice directly to Hu's residence. Hu opened the letter and learned about the matter. He immediately commissioned lawyer Fan Gang to report to the Old Zhabei Police Station. Detective Kraiden went to the Zhejiang Industrial Bank and opened safe deposit box number 401. The important gold jewelry was gone, and only miscellaneous items worth five to six hundred yuan were found. They were taken back to the police station. Yesterday morning, the items were sent to the Second Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Police lawyer Zhang Zhu Chenming explained the situation, stating that the complainant, Hu Boyi, was on his way from Nanchang to Shanghai and that Ai-ru had not yet been apprehended. He requested permission to temporarily store the seized items at the police station. Judge Yinghua immediately approved, instructing that the seized items be temporarily stored at the police station according to the inventory.

Workers and Shoemakers Feud, Gathering Crowds and Wielding Weapons

Xu Dechao Violently Pushed a Western Constable

Mastermind Gu Shuliang Arrested

Xu Shanjin, a leather shoemaker from Sicang Lane, Tokyo Road, West Shanghai, has a stall repairing leather shoes there. On the 27th of last month, Gu Shuliang, an Anhui worker from Maofeng Flour Mill at 25 Moganshan Road, brought two pairs of leather shoes to be repaired. At the time, the price was set at 12 cents. On the 30th, when Gu went to Xu's stall to pick up the shoes, he only offered 11 cents. Xu refused, leading to an argument and then a fight. Gu was beaten and injured in the eye. The police arrived and took both parties to the police station, where they were each fined 5 cents. As a result, Gu harbored resentment and sought revenge. He gathered fellow workers from the mill, about three to four hundred people, and on the afternoon of the day before yesterday, at 1:45 PM, they each carried real knives, guns, iron bars, and wooden rulers, preparing to cause trouble for Xu Shanjin. However, because there were so many people, the commotion reached the lane, and the Putuo Road Police Station was informed. Fearing a large-scale riot, the station immediately ordered constable number 25 and Chinese constables numbers 3879 and 2271, among others, to rush to Macau Road and Moganshan Road by motorcycle to suppress the crowd. When the crowd saw the Chinese and Western constables, they fled in all directions. However, Xu Dechao and Liu Wenxiu, natives of Anhui, were fearless and dared to resist. Xu violently pushed the Western constable, and Liu pulled out a bayonet to attack. Fortunately, the blade was blunt and only cut the leather glove, so no injury was sustained. As a result, in addition to Xu and Liu being arrested, accomplices Cai Zichu and Zhang Rongzhang were also apprehended. Cai was holding a long gun, and Zhang was holding a wooden stick. They were all taken to the police station and detained. They confessed that Gu was the mastermind. Detective lawyer Zhang Tianyin of the Eighth Criminal Court of the First Special District Court presented the case. Xu Shanjin and his apprentice Li Chunshan also filed a report, proving everything. When questioned, the defendants were evasive and hired lawyer Fan Gang to defend them. Judge Liu Yugui reviewed the confession and ordered Gu, Xu, and Liu to be remanded in custody. Cai and Zhang were each released on 100 yuan bail pending sentencing.

Apprentice Died Tragically After Being Pushed into the Huangpu River

The District Court Prosecutor's Office Clearly Filed a Public Prosecution After Investigation

Witness Testimony Vividly Depicted the Scene of Being Pushed into the River

The Deceased's Family Filed a Private Prosecution, and the Hearing Concluded Yesterday

Xu Binrong, a native of Yin County, Ningbo, is 58 years old and has only one son, Yisheng, 18 years old. Through an introduction, Yisheng became an apprentice at the Hetai Lumber Company on Caishi Road in the French Concession. On October 24 of this year, he was sent by the company to Taikoo Wharf in Pudong to deliver goods. After finishing the work, he intended to return to the company on the Taikoo Yangxing's fast ferry. Somehow, Xu Yisheng fell into the Huangpu River and drowned. At the time, Luo Xiaogou, a sailor on the ferry, reported to the water police station that the deceased had jumped into the river to commit suicide. However, witnesses who were present at the time greatly disagreed, claiming that the deceased had actually been pushed into the river by Luo Xiaogou and tragically drowned, and they were willing to testify. The water police station detained Luo Xiaogou and the captain of the ferry, Cao Zhangbao, and sent them to the District Court. Prosecutor Wu Deying conducted a clear investigation and filed a public prosecution against Luo Xiaogou and others on charges of homicide.

The victim's father, Xu Baorong, hired lawyer Zhang Ji to file a private prosecution, stating that Baorong was old and unable to work, and his only hope for support was his son Yisheng. Moreover, he had only this one son. Now, due to the defendants' cruel actions, Baorong's family had lost their source of support. Yisheng had received a middle school education and was about to complete his apprenticeship. Soon, he would be earning a monthly salary of 40 yuan. Baorong's family's monthly expenses for food and lodging were 25 yuan, which amounted to 300 yuan per year. The defendants should be jointly and severally liable to pay 5,000 yuan in compensation. Furthermore, calculating Yisheng's salary of 40 yuan per month from the age of 18 until he reached the age of 60, the compensation should be 20,160 yuan. The total compensation for the two items above should be 25,160 yuan. It was also stated that water and fire were merciless, and even women and children knew that every year, hundreds of people drowned in the Huangpu River. Moreover, the accident occurred on September 17 of the lunar calendar, during the afternoon high tide. That day, the north wind was howling, and there were turbulent waves. Luo Xiaogou was relying on his service to British expatriates and claiming to have foreign support, so he dared to act so recklessly. His heart was more vicious than a snake or a scorpion. The defendant, Cao Zhangbao, was the captain and in charge of the entire ferry. He was steering the ship. He could not claim ignorance and should have stopped the ship to rescue the person. He was truly culpable. Yesterday morning at 10 AM, Judge Sun Ji publicly heard the case in the Fifth Court. Luo Xiaogou, who was in custody, was brought to the case. He stated that he was 27 years old and a sailor on the fast ferry. Only those with passes were allowed to take the ferry to Pudong. On October 24, at about 10 AM, the deceased was about to jump off the gangway onto the ferry. He accidentally fell into the river. When asked if he had asked for a pass (i.e., a free ticket), he replied that he had not. He stated that the ship was casting off at the time. When asked how far the ship was from the dock at that time, he replied about four feet. When it was said that people on the shore said that he had asked the deceased for a pass and that because the deceased did not have a pass, he had pushed him into the river, he replied that the person selling noodles on the shore had a grudge against him. When asked if Cao Zhangbao had seen someone fall into the water, he replied that the captain had to pay attention to the outside of the ship when it was starting, so he did not see it. Cao Zhangbao stated that he was 49 years old, from Shanghai, and lived in Zhongshi, Yangjiadu, Guidong. He was the captain of the fast ferry. When asked how Xu Yisheng had fallen into the river, he replied that he had not seen it. When asked why he did not stop the engine when someone fell into the river, he replied that he heard shouts from the shore and immediately ordered a sailor to use a pole to rescue the person, but it was too late. Xu Baorong stated that he was 58 years old and that Yisheng was his son. On the day in question, he was planning to take the fast ferry, but because he did not have a pass, he was pushed into the Huangpu River and drowned by Luo Xiaogou. He requested justice. When asked if he had seen it, he replied that he had not. He was in Ningbo when he received a telegram from the company, and he rushed to Shanghai. Witness Qu Genfu stated that he was 35 years old, from Jiangbei, and made a living selling noodles on the floating bridge at Pier No. 3 of Huatong in Pudong. When asked if he had seen someone fall into the river, he replied that he had. When asked how he had seen it, he replied that the gentleman (the deceased) had eaten a bowl of noodles at his stall and boarded the ship. When asked if he had completely disembarked with both feet, he replied that his left foot was on the edge of the ship, and his right foot had not yet stepped on it. When asked if he lost his balance and fell into the river, he replied that he did not. When he boarded the ship, the sailor asked for a pass. Because he did not have a pass, he wanted to return to shore, but the sailor pushed him into the river. When asked how he could see so clearly, he replied that when he boarded the ship, he took a lead bucket to the river to fetch water. When asked how far he was from the ship when he was fetching water, he replied about a丈. Witness Jiang Lingen stated that he was 25 years old, from Tongzhou, and lived with Qu Genfu at the same noodle stall. The rest of his testimony was the same as Qu Genfu's, and he vividly described how the deceased boarded the ship and how he fell into the water. Witness Du Jinfu stated that he was 34 years old, from Shanghai, and worked at the Jianghai Customs. On the day in question, he was taking the ferry from Pudong back to Puxi. He witnessed the deceased running from the shore and jumping onto the ferry, lost his balance, and fell into the river. When asked if the sailor Luo Gou had asked for a pass, he replied that he had not. When asked how far the ship was from the dock, he replied about four feet. Witness Yan Changgen stated that he was 24 years old, from Shanghai, and worked as a shoe dealer. On the day in question, he was also taking the ferry to sell shoes. He witnessed the deceased falling into the river on his own. Witness Xu Xiting stated that he was 40 years old, from Nanjing, and worked in the rope business. He was standing on the dock waiting for another ship and also saw the deceased falling into the Huangpu River on his own. At this point, prosecutor Wu presented his arguments, and then the defense began. The lawyer hired by the defendant rose to defend for a long time. Lawyer Zhang, the plaintiff's private prosecutor, requested to pursue the private prosecution. The judge considered the case closed and scheduled the sentencing for 10 AM on the 10th of this month. Cao Zhangbao, who had previously been released on 300 yuan bail, had his bail increased by 1,000 yuan. Luo Xiaogou was remanded in custody pending instructions.

Zhang Jingou Returned to China Yesterday After Inspecting Plant Diseases and Pests

Implementation of Inspection Will Begin Next Month

The Ministry of Industry, recognizing that all countries attach great importance to the inspection of plant diseases and pests, specifically established a bureau to manage the inspection. However, China lacked such a system, so it drafted detailed measures, submitted them to the Executive Yuan for approval, and launched a pilot program. It also specifically sent Zhang Jingou, director of the plant disease and pest inspection team of the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau, to Japan, the South Seas Islands, and Taiwan to inspect and liaise with the relevant authorities in various countries to facilitate the inspection. Zhang returned to China yesterday. According to Zhang, during his trip abroad, he met with the inspection authorities in Japan, Taiwan, the South Seas Islands, and other places to discuss the inspection of plant diseases and pests and the facilitation of the inspection. The results were very satisfactory. The inspection systems in various countries are also very comprehensive and can serve as a reference for China. As for when China will implement plant disease and pest inspection, there are still various preparations to be made, so it will be difficult to implement it this month. It is expected to be implemented around January of next year.

German Consul-General in Shanghai, Kriebel, to Visit Wang Jingwei in Nanjing

Will Get off the Train in Zhenjiang for Sightseeing

According to the German Consulate, German Consul-General in Shanghai, Kriebel, left Shanghai on the 11:00 PM express train to Nanjing the day before yesterday (3rd) with four translators. Kriebel's trip is said to be to meet with Wang Jingwei, who is also the Minister of Foreign Affairs, to discuss Sino-German relations and trade issues. However, Kriebel will not travel directly to Nanjing. Because he has long admired the scenic spots of Jinshan and Jiaoshan in Zhenjiang, he will get off the train in Zhenjiang and stay for a day or two before continuing to Nanjing. He is expected to return to Shanghai around Monday or Tuesday of next week.

The Local Association Elected Its President Yesterday

Du Yuesheng and Qian Xinzhi Elected as President and Vice President

The Shanghai Local Association held an emergency meeting of its members at 6 PM yesterday. Fifty-two members attended. Chairman Wang Xiaolai announced the agenda. The first item was to commemorate Chairman Shi. Everyone stood up and observed three minutes of silence to express their grief. Then, he reported on the association's work and proposed various motions. After that, the election of the president was held. Du Yuesheng received 44 votes and was elected. Then, the election of the vice president was held. Qian Xinzhi received 38 votes and was elected. The audience applauded thunderously. The chairman replaced the vacant position of director left by Li Bu with alternate director Feng Bingnan. Everyone agreed. Then, Pang Jingzhou reported on the rescue team's work in Guangchang, the situation in which Chiang Kai-shek sent a telegram requesting them to continue their work, and the situation in which the party, government, and military officials in Guangchang sent telegrams requesting them to stay. It was decided to continue the work immediately, and the attendees made immediate donations, totaling over 9,000 yuan. It was already 7 PM, and the meeting adjourned.

Excellent Collection Results of the Travel Industry Aviation Donation Last Month

According to the Central News Agency, after the Shanghai Travel Industry's results in collecting the National Salvation Donation for Travel and Aviation were compiled by the Office of the General Team Leader of the Aviation Association and published in the newspapers last month, it aroused the attention and competition of the travel industry. A small number of travel businesses that were hesitant have begun to automatically implement the collection, and those that had already started but were not serious have increased their efforts. Therefore, the results for this month have increased by 20-30% compared to the previous period. It can be seen that the National Salvation Donation for Travel and Aviation will be more enthusiastic in the future, and it will not be difficult to complete the travel industry airplane within the shortest period. It is understood that the donation has been extracted by Zhang Yuliang from the office. To ensure that all sectors understand the donation, it is stipulated that it will be published once a month. The Water Level in Changyuan Has Dropped Compared to Before

According to a message from the Nanjing Industrial Relief Group, it was previously reported that the flood in Changyuan was severe, and the entire city was in danger of being submerged. The provincial government reported the situation to the central government. The Industrial Relief Group sent personnel to investigate. According to a telegram from Sang Zhetong and Wang Youlong, inspectors stationed in Changyuan, they were ordered to inquire about the reported situation that the water outside the city of Changyuan was one zhang higher than the water inside the city, the city walls were damaged, and there was a danger of submersion. They immediately telegraphed Zhang, the county magistrate of Changyuan, who replied that there was no such thing and that he had not reported it. The current water level has dropped by more than one chi and five cun compared to before. The newspaper reports were purely rumors. This information is specially disclosed to clarify the truth. It is also reported that the group received a telegram from Director Hua of the Hebei River Affairs Bureau, stating that the east dam of the Jiugulu No. 20 Koumen had been reinforced and raised by seven meters, and another section had been built with a length of seven meters, a width of seven meters, and a height of two meters and eight cun. The west dam was reinforced and extended by eleven meters and four cun, a width of seven meters, and a height of one meter and six cun today. It is also reported that inspectors Liu Bingzhong and Ye Jingyuan, stationed in Guantai, telegraphed that the east dam of Guantai had been reinforced with a length of seven zhang and a width of two zhang, and a height of six chi. The soil behind the dam had a length of seven zhang and a width of two zhang, and rose two chi above the water surface, totaling twenty-seven zhang and five chi. The weather was sunny and warm, 46 degrees, and the river level was stable. The construction at both locations is proceeding rapidly, and the blocking of the breaches is going smoothly. It is also reported that Kong Rong, director of the Industrial Relief Group, took the night train to Shanghai the day before yesterday (29th) to discuss industrial affairs with Secretary-General Zeng of the Huangzai Association General Office. The letter requesting the Henan Provincial Government to assist in repairing the water barrier dam built by the Chinese and Foreign Famine Relief Committee behind Guantai, which had been destroyed by the water, was prepared and brought to Beijing last night. It will be transferred to Bian for discussion and implementation to facilitate the work at the Koumen in Jiugulu and other places and to close the breaches as soon as possible.

The Shanghai National Products Company Scheduled to Establish a New Life Entertainment

The Shanghai National Products Company is the first national products store in Shanghai. It has spared no effort in promoting national products and urging the use of national products. It is scheduled to hold a winter sale and create a new life of entertainment starting on the 7th of this month. The instrument used is the High Blood Wealth Transformation Chart, based on "Propriety, Justice, Integrity, and Honor" and "Public Loyalty, Filial Piety, Brotherly Love, Diligence, Caution, Love, Benevolence, Wisdom, Gentleness, Kindness, Humility, Wisdom, Courage, Faith, and Peace." Entertainment rules are set, and anyone who purchases more than two yuan worth of goods can participate in the entertainment, and everyone can receive excellent gifts. Those who can win the four characters of Propriety, Justice, Humility, and Honor or a complete phrase such as Public Loyalty, Filial Piety, and Virtuous Brother on the same day will receive an additional valuable fur robe worth 100 gold.

Famous Music Band Hired from Vienna

Vienna Dance Hall on Jing'an Temple Road and Dahua Road is richly decorated and perfectly equipped. Chen Zhanxiong, the manager of the hall, hired the famous musician Mr. Pan Ganbeni at great expense to stimulate the interest of dancers. He has been performing in the hall since the day before yesterday. It is said that the musician has never performed in a Chinese dance hall before, making this truly the first time.

Compilation of Bank Inspection Reports

The Reserve of the Four Banks is jointly established by the Yanye, Jincheng, Zhongnan, and Continental Banks to exclusively handle the issuance of banknotes for the Zhongnan Bank. According to the bank's issuance charter, banknotes are issued with full reserves, with a minimum of 60% cash reserves and a maximum of 40% guarantee reserves. A public announcement is made every week, and it is audited by the auditors and accountants of the four banks. The 257th public announcement of the Shanghai Reserve Hall on December 1, 23, is recorded below: Amount of banknotes in circulation: 31,464,573 yuan Total amount of reserves: 31,464,573 yuan, including: Cash reserves: 24,157,923 yuan Guarantee reserves: 7,306,650 yuan

The November 30 inspection report of the Issuance Reserve of Siming Bank states that the bank's banknotes are issued with full reserves, with a minimum of 60% cash reserves and a maximum of 40% guarantee reserves. The inspection report by accountants Wu Hui and Pan Zhaobang, and supervisors Xiang Fenglou and Xu Boxiong, is as follows: Total amount of exchange certificates issued: 17,600,600 yuan Total amount of reserves: 17,600,600 yuan, including: The bank's own issuance: 10,800,600 yuan Reserves: 9,110,600 yuan in cash, 1,690,000 yuan in guarantees Amount received by peers: 6,800,000 yuan Reserves: 4,580,000 yuan in cash, 2,220,000 yuan in guarantees Accountants Wu Zheng and Pan Zhaobang, supervisors Xiang Fenglou and Xu Boxiong.

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the weather in Shandong, the middle and lower reaches of the Yangtze River is clear and cold. Strong winds are coming from the northwest to the northeast. The East China Sea and the Taiwan Strait are mostly cloudy with rain in some places. The north to northeast winds are very strong. The weather between the Ryukyu Islands and the Ogasawara Islands is very bad due to a hurricane passing through and moving northeast. The hurricane south of Macclesfield Island is slowly dissipating. The first hurricane center was located at 2 PM within 60 miles of 14 degrees north latitude and 130 degrees east longitude, moving northeast with strong winds. The second hurricane center was located at 2 PM within 120 miles of 10 degrees north latitude and 142 degrees east longitude, moving west-northwest with weak winds. Before 1 PM yesterday, the temperature in the city in the past 24 hours was a maximum of 50.1 and a minimum of 23.8. On the same day last year, the maximum was 65.8 and the minimum was 37.4.

Sincerely,

Jiaotong University

An investigation of the daily foreign exchange rates in the past month (November) showed that the first half of the month was not very expensive, but the second half of the month suddenly exceeded the significant range, as high as four corners, and the total statistics for the entire month were over 5.6 yuan. Since the base of the interest rate was large, the negotiation price also increased. The Standing Committee of the Money Industry Association decided the other day that the interest rate was 5.595 yuan, which was a world of difference compared to the October market price, which was 2 yuan. In this case, the interest market price has exceeded the fixed settlement price of 4.5 yuan, so this time the interest will inevitably increase, with the highest interest generally being around 12 yuan. Securities Debt market trends are softening. Unfounded rumors are lightly shrouded. Down two to four jiao. Yesterday's trend on the Chinese Securities Exchange was hovering and weak. After many days of gains, there was a small pause. It was a matter of expectations that the foreign exchange rate fell to two and a half jiao and the head and tail did not match. It seemed that the money market had loosened. However, the market price was weak, which was beyond some people's expectations. In fact, there were too many long positions. There are two common concepts in long positions' psychology: one is that the Fifth National Congress will definitely be held as scheduled, and the market price will definitely rise after the meeting; the other is that the market price is still far from the previous peak, and the salt tax and unified tax have increased the number of repayments starting in February. All kinds of situations are beneficial to long positions, so those who take long positions are very active, and they are all going long in the future. Therefore, the forward market prices of each debt market are almost equal to this month. In the past, when there were occasional phenomena like this, it would cause arbitrage transactions and pull the market to level. This phenomenon has been going on for many days, but arbitrage is not possible. It can be seen that the money market has not yet loosened. However, the recent need for cash has been rare, so the foreign exchange rate has returned to low levels. The future of the market price is likely to be hovering and weak for the time being. Yesterday's experience was that although the foreign exchange rate continued to fall, the opening market price fell immediately. The disarmament was more than half a yuan lower. Long positions were too eager, and this was even more convincing. After entering the 23rd pass, it recovered slightly. Amateur Mailbox

My Family Won't Let Me Continue My Education

Editor:

I have a question about lifelong learning that I would like you to give me a satisfactory answer to.

I am a junior high school student about to graduate, and based on my family's financial situation, I still have the possibility of entering high school. However, judging from my father's recent intentions, he is unwilling to let me continue studying. He hopes that after I graduate, he can find something for me to do, which will not only reduce a large sum of money from the family, but may also be able to subsidize the household a bit. But I myself feel that my knowledge is very shallow and not enough to cope with everything in society, and in this era of extremely high unemployment, with my junior high school qualifications, what good job can I find? Therefore, for my future happiness, I have decided to request to continue my education in order to seek higher learning. So in the past two days, I have talked to my family several times, asking them to satisfy my desire for education. But they have very firmly and stubbornly refused my request. As a result, there is a conflict of opinion between me and my family. I originally wanted to break with them, but then I thought that after the break, the source of economic support would be cut off. Then, not only would I not be able to study, but I would not even be able to maintain my personal life. But if I just give in to my family and stop studying after graduation, I feel that the future is too hopeless and life is too meaningless. So now I think that if I can't achieve my goal, I might as well just die, so as not to suffer in the future. Sir, you are a guiding needle in my lost way. In my situation, what should I do? I respectfully hope for your answer. With best wishes for your well-being.

Editor's Note:

The reason why most people cannot continue their education is due to financial difficulties. It seems too rare and too stubborn that Ji Jun's family has the financial ability to provide their children with continued education, but they ignore Ji Jun's future happiness and resolutely ask him to stop studying and find a job. Now, based on the meaning of the letter, the editor has assumed several steps for your reference. ㈠ First, ask relatives and friends to find a way to gently discuss with your family, hoping that they can change their prejudices and allow your request. ㈡ If they definitely do not agree, then you can only plead with your family again, or argue with them, and insist on your determination to continue your education. When they are too annoyed, they may allow you to do so. ㈢ Suicide is the behavior of the weak. I hope you don't think of death just because you can't go to school, but when there is no room for redemption, you might as well use [death] to threaten your family. We think that elders always love their children, and they will never let you die. So if you demand it with your life, then you can finally achieve your goal. If you have other opportunities for borrowing or work-study, that would be even better, and you won't have to ask your family. Finally, the editor believes that all kinds of knowledge are not limited to what can be obtained in schools. A person has the opportunity to study anytime and anywhere. Serving is also studying, and we believe that only practical life experience is real knowledge. However, these words are for those who are unable to enter school to study. If they have the ability, of course it is better to go to school to study.

Opening [Sweeping Qin]

Don't laugh at my crazy, foolish appearance. The Earth Store Bodhisattva intentionally descends to the mortal world. He sits in meditation in the Lingyin Temple. He blesses the virtuous father and son of the Yue family to ascend to the immortal realm as soon as possible. He suddenly sees the poem and the treacherous hero trembles in fear. This poem is written with his wife. The incident is revealed and a fire starts. He immediately shouts angrily at the crazy monk. He doesn't know that he is full of Zen and can change in many ways. He can summon wind and rain. He holds a fire tube to communicate with foreign countries. He also takes a palm broom to sweep away treacherous officials. The storm is only caused by monopolizing power. He dies unjustly in the Cold Spring Pavilion. Chinese Classics

Ms. Wang Bingmei's Tang Poetry

Huaxing (1260) 9:00 AM to 10:00 AM

The Ballad of the Army Carts Du Fu

The chariots rumble, the horses neigh,

The conscripts each carry bows and arrows at their waist.

Fathers, mothers, wives, and children run to see them off,

Their forms disappear in the dust beyond Xianyang Bridge.

Pulling at clothes, stamping feet, they cry and block the road,

Their wails reach the high heavens.

A passerby asks a conscript,

The conscript says only that the conscription is frequent.

Some from fifteen north to defend the river,

Then to forty west to garrison the fields.

When they left, the village head wrapped their heads,

Returning with white hair, they still defend the border.

The blood flows at the border to form a sea,

The Emperor Wu's intention to expand the border is not yet finished.

Have you not heard that of the Han family's two hundred prefectures east of the mountains,

Thousands of villages grow thorns and reeds?

Even if there are strong women holding plows,

The wheat grows east and west in the fields.

Moreover, the Qin soldiers endure bitter battles,

Driven no differently than dogs and chickens.

Although the elders have hatred,

How dare the conscripts express their hatred?

Moreover, this year there are many

Unfinished levies in Guanzhong.

The county officials urgently demand rent,

From where can the rent and taxes come?

Believe me, it is evil to give birth to a son,

It is better to give birth to a daughter.

A daughter can still be married to a neighbor,

A son is buried and buried in the wilderness.

Have you not seen the shores of Qinghai?

Since ancient times, the white bones have been uncollected.

New ghosts worry the old ghosts,

When the sky is overcast and the rain is wet, their voices cry out.

Shen Bao Local Supplement Film Special

Hollywood in the Midst of Recession

Su Hua

European Silver Star and Famous Director Hired by Fox

Curval Boedt and Eric Charell Worth Noting

The dense fog of recession is undeniably enveloping the globe. The extremely luxurious Hollywood also feels extreme unease. Smaller production companies with less capital have no choice but to stop working. And those famous film companies with strong capital and solid foundations, such as MGM, Paramount, RKO, and Fox, although they will not experience any [economic panic]; however, now they have to carefully calculate the expenditure for each film.

In this situation of economic tightening, Fox Company spared no expense to hire a European red star, Curval Boedt, and a famous director, Eric Charell, to Hollywood to join their ranks. Isn't this a very noteworthy thing?

Before we know why Fox Company spared no expense to hire these two artists, I should give the readers a brief introduction to them.

For Curval Boedt, I'm afraid most of us still feel very unfamiliar. This is because the films he starred in in Europe rarely come to Shanghai. He is a red-hot person on the stage in Europe, and also a bright and shining star on the screen. Now Fox Company has invited him to Hollywood, and the first film they gave him to star in is the musical epic [The Taming of the Shrew] made by Fox Company at a cost of millions of dollars (it is said that this film will be released in Shanghai).

Indeed, Curval Boedt has many things worth admiring. He has received a very good education. He is already married (the female lead in [Rembrandt] showing in Shanghai, Gertrude Michael). He has the gentleness of a poet and the healthy physique of a boxer. He is kind and courteous in dealing with people, and has never shown any unhappiness. In his half-open and half-closed eyes, he fully expresses the enthusiasm in his heart. Interestingly, the contours of his face are very similar to [famous comedian] Charlie Chaplin, and his actions also have similarities with Charlie Chaplin.

He was born with a very determined temperament. He must do well what he intends to do, without any doubt. He intended to practice English specially for two months before filming [The Taming of the Shrew] recently. Now his pronunciation is so accurate that it is beyond his own expectations. His only hobby is that he likes to smoke cigarettes very much. Outdoor sports are also his favorite. Skating can be said to be his forte. I'm afraid there are not many people in Hollywood who can compare with him in skating skills.

Famous director Eric Charell, I'm afraid everyone knows him. The world-praised [Congress Dances] is his production. Using music as the background and using music to harmonize the atmosphere in the play are his special skills and the success of his works. This time he came to Hollywood and directed Fox's million-dollar epic [The Taming of the Shrew]. We believe that Fox Company's sacrifice of a huge amount of money will definitely achieve considerable results.

The question is turned over again, now we must understand that film is a noble and conscious entertainment. It can provide people with knowledge, experience, comfort people's hearts, and make people forget temporary troubles. Therefore, even in the midst of the recession, noble and beneficial entertainment is still needed; in other words, people who are committed to the mission of the eighth art should provide people with some happiness as much as possible when the world is plunged into gloom, so that people's lives will not continue to be monotonous. Perhaps Fox Company's willingness to hire these two artists at no expense this time is based on this purpose.

Film Review

Review of [Female Prisoner] Jin Cheng Ling He

In any case, this film is one that we should earnestly discuss with the author, because from content to form, [Female Prisoner] is not a successful work.

First of all, we must say that the author's narrow concept of revenge inevitably plunges this film into the old quagmire. Naturally, the main reason for its failure is that the play cannot grasp the reality in the work, but is just fantasy and fiction. So when we watch this film, we only feel that we are listening to a story that is not related to our daily life, and of course it cannot arouse our true emotions.

Although we dare not say that [Female Prisoner] is a reflection of [petty bourgeois thought], the author's outdated ideas are undeniable. It is very clear that he used the means of flattering power to construct the so-called [revolution] story. But this explanation of [revolution] is ridiculous in any case. For example, is the daughter of the so-called [revolutionary] a revolutionary? No, she doesn't understand anything about national affairs at all, she only knows that the hatred of killing her father must be avenged, but the author says at the end that she is eliminating harm for the country. This is a far-fetched association for no reason in any case. As for the concept of personal revenge, it is even more unnecessary to explain.

On the playwright's side, perhaps he thinks that the enemy is the husband's father, and that killing the father-in-law for revenge is quite dramatic, but in our opinion, it is better to say that it is an impossible coincidence than a dramatic grasp. In fact, the playwright does not want her to marry the son of a fried dough stick seller, but wants her to combine with a young master, which shows his outdated ideas. Moreover, it is not a realistic stereotype that a young master would marry a wandering girl. As for the son not knowing his father's real name, and the real name being tattooed on his hand, but the son never discovered it, it is also unbelievable.

Furthermore, since the playwright thinks that the revenge scene is the highlight, we will not discuss whether it is correctly expressed for the time being. The playwright undoubtedly regards it as the climax of the whole play, but the result is that the director uses an extremely slow tone, and unnecessarily prolongs the time, resulting in not only a lack of tension, but also a feeling of unbearable dullness. It is conceivable that it is not a film technique.

Let's look at how the director portrays the characters in the play. This can be explained by taking the heroine as a representative. If she is to take on the heavy responsibility of revenge, then she should have the posture of a hero, but what is shown on the screen is that she not only does not have the spirit of a hero, but is a very mediocre woman. In addition, we don't need to go into detail about the unsuccessful acting skills.

Marlene Dietrich Buys Keys Donglin

[Could it be that she has found a lover?]

Recently, because Marlene Dietrich often goes to hardware stores to buy keys, people in Hollywood are looking at her with curious eyes.

Do you know why this is? It turns out that in Hollywood, if a woman gives a key to a man, it means [I can let you have everything [free]]. For this reason, when people see Marlene buying keys there, they all think that she must have found a lover.

But the strange thing is that Dietrich is always buying keys, but she has never seen the shadow of the [so-called lover]. So people have to wonder again.

A friend finally couldn't bear it anymore. One day, when he saw Dietrich, he immediately asked: [Why are you always buying keys?]

Marlene smiled and replied after hearing her friend's words: [Do you know that my daughter Maria is very naughty? When I'm not at home, she always takes the keys to who knows where, so I always have to get new keys!]

This mystery is finally broken!

The Capital Air Defense Exercise Was Filmed by Yihua

Yi

When the capital held a major air defense exercise on the 25th of last month, Yihua Company sent a large number of people to shoot news films in order to arouse the attention of the people to air defense. The directors included Zheng Yingshi, director of [Flying Flower Village], Shi Dongshan, director of [The Beginning of Man], Yuan Congmei, director of [The Sacrificer], and photographers Zhou Ke, Wang Yang, and photography assistants Tong Benkui and Han Zhongliang. Shi Dongshan and Zhou Ke specialized in shooting the fighting and competition of airplanes, Zheng Yingshi and Tong Benkui specialized in shooting the activities of anti-aircraft artillery teams, security teams, and fire brigades, and Yuan Congmei and Wang Yang specialized in shooting the work of maintaining law and order on the streets and obstacles. They ran around tirelessly. Sometimes they took airplanes together to shoot aerial combat scenes, sometimes they followed behind the fire brigade to shoot disaster relief situations, and sometimes they went back and forth between the anti-aircraft artillery team and the searchlight team to shoot real anti-aircraft artillery scenes. Therefore, when they came back, none of them were not as tired as cotton wool, but their harvest was really a lot.

Soviet Russia's Great Construction [Storm] Opens Today

[Storm] is a super-special production of the Soviet Russian Suki Film Company in 1934, starring the famous Soviet Russian female star Tarasava. The content tells the story of an orphan girl who, when she gets married, is blinded by her husband's family because she has no huge dowry. After various twists and turns, she finally throws herself into the river and dies. The plot is sad and gorgeous, and it is worthy of singing and weeping. Its exposure to the contradictions of life and the selfishness of human beings can be said to be complete. According to the original author of this film, it is the world-famous playwright Ostrovsky. Ostrovsky is good at depicting the dark side of social life in the old Russian era. This play is his masterpiece in his life. It has been staged many times in Europe before, and recently it was made into a film by Soviet Russia. On the day of its release in Soviet Russia, thousands of people flocked to it, which was very grand for a while, and its value can be imagined. Now the film has been decided to be released in Shanghai's Paris Grand Theater starting from the 5th of this month.

Film Novel

The Mother-Daughter Relationship (Lady by Cholce) (3) Zhong Jia

Panxi was startled when she heard the judge scolding her. She thought that the judge was always very kind, but why was he so strict this time? She only heard the judge say to the police officer who arrested her: [Take her down. I will consider it again for the time being. Second case!] When he shouted the second case, his voice was louder. Alaban looked at Panxi staggering and following the policeman out, and couldn't help feeling depressed. And the second case was hers. She originally listened to her manager Kendall and asked the police to bring her up in order to stir up public opinion as publicity. But now she was a little scared. She felt that the court was not a good place to play, and this time she was probably fooled by Kendall. After a while, when it was her turn to appear in court, she became even more afraid, because what she expected was not bad. Her pleas seemed to be blown away by the wind, and she couldn't hear them. Although according to her ideal, the statue in the art academy only covered her lower body with a fig leaf, and she was still covering herself with such a large ostrich feather fan. Unexpectedly, the judge gave her a long lecture. She still argued strongly: [My feather fan dance is not bad at all. I can dance it for you now. But you have to imagine all the lights and music……] As she spoke, she gently stretched out her wrist and untied her loose leather coat. The judge was startled when he saw it, even though he only saw a snow-white and tender shoulder. He immediately took the hammer, knocked on the public case and shouted: [No dancing! The court is a night court, not a nightclub! I now sentence you to one year of imprisonment on Black Well Island and a fine of one hundred yuan!] After he finished speaking, he saw infinite panic and grief suddenly appear on the woman's face. They thought that his heart was too hard. Or perhaps Panxi's case made him so angry. Because his kindness did not help Panxi, if Alaban was arrested for the first time and she was not severely punished, she would become Panxi the second in the future. Then his strictness was right, but when he looked at Alaban's face again, he felt unbearable again, because her face was full of an unimaginable sorrow, her lips were trembling, her eyes contained two bags of tears, and the child-like face could not be seen in the midnight court. In this way, he felt that perhaps he was too strict. So he involuntarily continued: [However, because you are in front of me for the first time, I can announce a suspended sentence. Do not commit the crime again next time. If you dance naked again, whether you have a feather fan or not, in short, it is to destroy the peace and morality of this city, and I will immediately execute the previous sentence. Second case!] In this way, he lightly dismissed Alaban. After he finished hearing several other cases and retired to the rest room, he was already exhausted. He saw Panxi was still waiting there, and there was still an empty wine bottle in the wastepaper basket, which was the case every time Panxi came here. At first, he was very unhappy, but soon he felt that he should understand her. He also felt sorry for her. At this time, he had to use strong wine to warm her heart and maintain her spirit. So he ordered the court clerk: [Quickly call Johnny Mills!] Panxi couldn't help but feel half a head shorter when she heard this. She originally hoped that Johnny would not know about this recent case. Johnny was instructed by his father a few years ago to look for her and take care of her. That was the last thing his father told him before he died. Johnny actually found her after listening to his father's words, but he had no way to take care of her. (To be continued)
